\enubox{\Large\bf Psalms}
\raisebox{16pt}{B516x512S14021485x488} \raisebox{20pt}{B508x508S20320493x493} \raisebox{20pt}{B510x508S1f720490x493} \raisebox{20pt}{B512x515S1dc20488x485} \raisebox{20pt}{B510x513S18d20490x488} \raisebox{20pt}{B508x508S20320493x493}

\begin{multicols}{2}


\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 1}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M508x515S10000493x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Blessed is the man that walketh not in the counsel of the ungodly, nor standeth in the way of sinners, nor sitteth in the seat of the scornful.}

\enubox{2 But his delight is in the law of the LORD; and in his law doth he meditate day and night.}

\enubox{3 And he shall be like a tree planted by the rivers of water, that bringeth forth his fruit in his season; his leaf also shall not wither; and whatsoever he doeth shall prosper.}

\enubox{4 The ungodly are not so: but are like the chaff which the wind driveth away.}

\enubox{5 Therefore the ungodly shall not stand in the judgment, nor sinners in the congregation of the righteous.}

\enubox{6 For the LORD knoweth the way of the righteous: but the way of the ungodly shall perish.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 2}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M508x515S10e00493x485 
\end{center}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 3}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Lord, how are they increased that trouble me! many are they that rise up against me.}

\enubox{2 Many there be which say of my soul, There is no help for him in God. Selah.}

\enubox{3 But thou, O LORD, art a shield for me; my glory, and the lifter up of mine head.}

\enubox{4 I cried unto the LORD with my voice, and he heard me out of his holy hill. Selah.}

\enubox{5 I laid me down and slept; I awaked; for the LORD sustained me.}

\enubox{6 I will not be afraid of ten thousands of people, that have set themselves against me round about.}

\enubox{7 Arise, O LORD; save me, O my God: for thou hast smitten all mine enemies upon the cheek bone; thou hast broken the teeth of the ungodly.}

\enubox{8 Salvation belongeth unto the LORD: thy blessing is upon thy people. Selah.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 4}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Hear me when I call, O God of my righteousness: thou hast enlarged me when I was in distress; have mercy upon me, and hear my prayer.}

\enubox{2 O ye sons of men, how long will ye turn my glory into shame? how long will ye love vanity, and seek after leasing? Selah.}

\enubox{3 But know that the LORD hath set apart him that is godly for himself: the LORD will hear when I call unto him.}

\enubox{4 Stand in awe, and sin not: commune with your own heart upon your bed, and be still. Selah.}

\enubox{5 Offer the sacrifices of righteousness, and put your trust in the LORD.}

\enubox{6 There be many that say, Who will shew us any good? LORD, lift thou up the light of thy countenance upon us.}

\enubox{7 Thou hast put gladness in my heart, more than in the time that their corn and their wine increased.}

\enubox{8 I will both lay me down in peace, and sleep: for thou, LORD, only makest me dwell in safety.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 5}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Give ear to my words, O LORD, consider my meditation.}

\enubox{2 Hearken unto the voice of my cry, my King, and my God: for unto thee will I pray.}

\enubox{3 My voice shalt thou hear in the morning, O LORD; in the morning will I direct my prayer unto thee, and will look up.}

\enubox{4 For thou art not a God that hath pleasure in wickedness: neither shall evil dwell with thee.}

\enubox{5 The foolish shall not stand in thy sight: thou hatest all workers of iniquity.}

\enubox{6 Thou shalt destroy them that speak leasing: the LORD will abhor the bloody and deceitful man.}

\enubox{7 But as for me, I will come into thy house in the multitude of thy mercy: and in thy fear will I worship toward thy holy temple.}

\enubox{8 Lead me, O LORD, in thy righteousness because of mine enemies; make thy way straight before my face.}

\enubox{9 For there is no faithfulness in their mouth; their inward part is very wickedness; their throat is an open sepulchre; they flatter with their tongue.}

\enubox{10 Destroy thou them, O God; let them fall by their own counsels; cast them out in the multitude of their transgressions; for they have rebelled against thee.}

\enubox{11 But let all those that put their trust in thee rejoice: let them ever shout for joy, because thou defendest them: let them also that love thy name be joyful in thee.}

\enubox{12 For thou, LORD, wilt bless the righteous; with favour wilt thou compass him as with a shield.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 6}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M509x515S18720491x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O LORD, rebuke me not in thine anger, neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.}

\enubox{2 Have mercy upon me, O LORD; for I am weak: O LORD, heal me; for my bones are vexed.}

\enubox{3 My soul is also sore vexed: but thou, O LORD, how long?}

\enubox{4 Return, O LORD, deliver my soul: oh save me for thy mercies' sake.}

\enubox{5 For in death there is no remembrance of thee: in the grave who shall give thee thanks?}

\enubox{6 I am weary with my groaning; all the night make I my bed to swim; I water my couch with my tears.}

\enubox{7 Mine eye is consumed because of grief; it waxeth old because of all mine enemies.}

\enubox{8 Depart from me, all ye workers of iniquity; for the LORD hath heard the voice of my weeping.}

\enubox{9 The LORD hath heard my supplication; the LORD will receive my prayer.}

\enubox{10 Let all mine enemies be ashamed and sore vexed: let them return and be ashamed suddenly.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 7}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x514S1a520490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O LORD my God, in thee do I put my trust: save me from all them that persecute me, and deliver me:}

\enubox{2 Lest he tear my soul like a lion, rending it in pieces, while there is none to deliver.}

\enubox{3 O LORD my God, If I have done this; if there be iniquity in my hands;}

\enubox{4 If I have rewarded evil unto him that was at peace with me; (yea, I have delivered him that without cause is mine enemy:)}

\enubox{5 Let the enemy persecute my soul, and take it; yea, let him tread down my life upon the earth, and lay mine honour in the dust. Selah.}

\enubox{6 Arise, O LORD, in thine anger, lift up thyself because of the rage of mine enemies: and awake for me to the judgment that thou hast commanded.}

\enubox{7 So shall the congregation of the people compass thee about: for their sakes therefore return thou on high.}

\enubox{8 The LORD shall judge the people: judge me, O LORD, according to my righteousness, and according to mine integrity that is in me.}

\enubox{9 Oh let the wickedness of the wicked come to an end; but establish the just: for the righteous God trieth the hearts and reins.}

\enubox{10 My defence is of God, which saveth the upright in heart.}

\enubox{11 God judgeth the righteous, and God is angry with the wicked every day.}

\enubox{12 If he turn not, he will whet his sword; he hath bent his bow, and made it ready.}

\enubox{13 He hath also prepared for him the instruments of death; he ordaineth his arrows against the persecutors.}

\enubox{14 Behold, he travaileth with iniquity, and hath conceived mischief, and brought forth falsehood.}

\enubox{15 He made a pit, and digged it, and is fallen into the ditch which he made.}

\enubox{16 His mischief shall return upon his own head, and his violent dealing shall come down upon his own pate.}

\enubox{17 I will praise the LORD according to his righteousness: and will sing praise to the name of the LORD most high.}

\enubox{1 O LORD, our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth! who hast set thy glory above the heavens.}

\enubox{2 Out of the mouth of babes and sucklings hast thou ordained strength because of thine enemies, that thou mightest still the enemy and the avenger.}

\enubox{3 When I consider thy heavens, the work of thy fingers, the moon and the stars, which thou hast ordained;}

\enubox{4 What is man, that thou art mindful of him? and the son of man, that thou visitest him?}

\enubox{7 All sheep and oxen, yea, and the beasts of the field;}

\enubox{8 The fowl of the air, and the fish of the sea, and whatsoever passeth through the paths of the seas.}

\enubox{9 O LORD our Lord, how excellent is thy name in all the earth!}

\enubox{\bf Chapter 9}

\enubox{1 I will praise thee, O LORD, with my whole heart; I will shew forth all thy marvellous works.}

\enubox{2 I will be glad and rejoice in thee: I will sing praise to thy name, O thou most High.}

\enubox{3 When mine enemies are turned back, they shall fall and perish at thy presence.}

\enubox{4 For thou hast maintained my right and my cause; thou satest in the throne judging right.}

\enubox{5 Thou hast rebuked the heathen, thou hast destroyed the wicked, thou hast put out their name for ever and ever.}

\enubox{6 O thou enemy, destructions are come to a perpetual end: and thou hast destroyed cities; their memorial is perished with them.}

\enubox{7 But the LORD shall endure for ever: he hath prepared his throne for judgment.}

\enubox{8 And he shall judge the world in righteousness, he shall minister judgment to the people in uprightness.}

\enubox{9 The LORD also will be a refuge for the oppressed, a refuge in times of trouble.}

\enubox{10 And they that know thy name will put their trust in thee: for thou, LORD, hast not forsaken them that seek thee.}

\enubox{11 Sing praises to the LORD, which dwelleth in Zion: declare among the people his doings.}

\enubox{12 When he maketh inquisition for blood, he remembereth them: he forgetteth not the cry of the humble.}

\enubox{13 Have mercy upon me, O LORD; consider my trouble which I suffer of them that hate me, thou that liftest me up from the gates of death:}

\enubox{14 That I may shew forth all thy praise in the gates of the daughter of Zion: I will rejoice in thy salvation.}

\enubox{15 The heathen are sunk down in the pit that they made: in the net which they hid is their own foot taken.}

\enubox{16 The LORD is known by the judgment which he executeth: the wicked is snared in the work of his own hands. Higgaion. Selah.}

\enubox{17 The wicked shall be turned into hell, and all the nations that forget God.}

\enubox{18 For the needy shall not alway be forgotten: the expectation of the poor shall not perish for ever.}

\enubox{19 Arise, O LORD; let not man prevail: let the heathen be judged in thy sight.}

\enubox{20 Put them in fear, O LORD: that the nations may know themselves to be but men. Selah.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 10}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M513x528S2a538494x472S1f540488x504 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Why standest thou afar off, O LORD? why hidest thou thyself in times of trouble?}

\enubox{2 The wicked in his pride doth persecute the poor: let them be taken in the devices that they have imagined.}

\enubox{3 For the wicked boasteth of his heart's desire, and blesseth the covetous, whom the LORD abhorreth.}

\enubox{4 The wicked, through the pride of his countenance, will not seek after God: God is not in all his thoughts.}

\enubox{5 His ways are always grievous; thy judgments are far above out of his sight: as for all his enemies, he puffeth at them.}

\enubox{6 He hath said in his heart, I shall not be moved: for I shall never be in adversity.}

\enubox{7 His mouth is full of cursing and deceit and fraud: under his tongue is mischief and vanity.}

\enubox{8 He sitteth in the lurking places of the villages: in the secret places doth he murder the innocent: his eyes are privily set against the poor.}

\enubox{9 He lieth in wait secretly as a lion in his den: he lieth in wait to catch the poor: he doth catch the poor, when he draweth him into his net.}

\enubox{10 He croucheth, and humbleth himself, that the poor may fall by his strong ones.}

\enubox{11 He hath said in his heart, God hath forgotten: he hideth his face; he will never see it.}

\enubox{12 Arise, O LORD; O God, lift up thine hand: forget not the humble.}

\enubox{13 Wherefore doth the wicked contemn God? he hath said in his heart, Thou wilt not require it.}

\enubox{14 Thou hast seen it; for thou beholdest mischief and spite, to requite it with thy hand: the poor committeth himself unto thee; thou art the helper of the fatherless.}

\enubox{15 Break thou the arm of the wicked and the evil man: seek out his wickedness till thou find none.}

\enubox{16 The LORD is King for ever and ever: the heathen are perished out of his land.}

\enubox{17 LORD, thou hast heard the desire of the humble: thou wilt prepare their heart, thou wilt cause thine ear to hear:}

\enubox{18 To judge the fatherless and the oppressed, that the man of the earth may no more oppress.}

\enubox{1 In the LORD put I my trust: how say ye to my soul, Flee as a bird to your mountain?}

\enubox{2 For, lo, the wicked bend their bow, they make ready their arrow upon the string, that they may privily shoot at the upright in heart.}

\enubox{3 If the foundations be destroyed, what can the righteous do?}

\enubox{4 The LORD is in his holy temple, the LORD's throne is in heaven: his eyes behold, his eyelids try, the children of men.}

\enubox{5 The LORD trieth the righteous: but the wicked and him that loveth violence his soul hateth.}

\enubox{6 Upon the wicked he shall rain snares, fire and brimstone, and an horrible tempest: this shall be the portion of their cup.}

\enubox{7 For the righteous LORD loveth righteousness; his countenance doth behold the upright.}

\enubox{3 The LORD shall cut off all flattering lips, and the tongue that speaketh proud things:}

\enubox{4 Who have said, With our tongue will we prevail; our lips are our own: who is lord over us?}

\enubox{5 For the oppression of the poor, for the sighing of the needy, now will I arise, saith the LORD; I will set him in safety from him that puffeth at him.}

\enubox{6 The words of the LORD are pure words: as silver tried in a furnace of earth, purified seven times.}

\enubox{7 Thou shalt keep them, O LORD, thou shalt preserve them from this generation for ever.}

\enubox{8 The wicked walk on every side, when the vilest men are exalted.}

\enubox{3 Thou hast proved mine heart; thou hast visited me in the night; thou hast tried me, and shalt find nothing; I am purposed that my mouth shall not transgress.}

\enubox{5 Hold up my goings in thy paths, that my footsteps slip not.}

\enubox{6 I have called upon thee, for thou wilt hear me, O God: incline thine ear unto me, and hear my speech.}

\enubox{7 Shew thy marvellous lovingkindness, O thou that savest by thy right hand them which put their trust in thee from those that rise up against them.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 18}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M523x522S1bb00502x492S2e00e478x479 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I will love thee, O LORD, my strength.}

\enubox{2 The LORD is my rock, and my fortress, and my deliverer; my God, my strength, in whom I will trust; my buckler, and the horn of my salvation, and my high tower.}

\enubox{3 I will call upon the LORD, who is worthy to be praised: so shall I be saved from mine enemies.}

\enubox{4 The sorrows of death compassed me, and the floods of ungodly men made me afraid.}

\enubox{5 The sorrows of hell compassed me about: the snares of death prevented me.}

\enubox{6 In my distress I called upon the LORD, and cried unto my God: he heard my voice out of his temple, and my cry came before him, even into his ears.}

\enubox{7 Then the earth shook and trembled; the foundations also of the hills moved and were shaken, because he was wroth.}

\enubox{8 There went up a smoke out of his nostrils, and fire out of his mouth devoured: coals were kindled by it.}

\enubox{9 He bowed the heavens also, and came down: and darkness was under his feet.}

\enubox{10 And he rode upon a cherub, and did fly: yea, he did fly upon the wings of the wind.}

\enubox{11 He made darkness his secret place; his pavilion round about him were dark waters and thick clouds of the skies.}

\enubox{12 At the brightness that was before him his thick clouds passed, hail stones and coals of fire.}

\enubox{13 The LORD also thundered in the heavens, and the Highest gave his voice; hail stones and coals of fire.}

\enubox{14 Yea, he sent out his arrows, and scattered them; and he shot out lightnings, and discomfited them.}

\enubox{15 Then the channels of waters were seen, and the foundations of the world were discovered at thy rebuke, O LORD, at the blast of the breath of thy nostrils.}

\enubox{16 He sent from above, he took me, he drew me out of many waters.}

\enubox{17 He delivered me from my strong enemy, and from them which hated me: for they were too strong for me.}

\enubox{18 They prevented me in the day of my calamity: but the LORD was my stay.}

\enubox{19 He brought me forth also into a large place; he delivered me, because he delighted in me.}

\enubox{20 The LORD rewarded me according to my righteousness; according to the cleanness of my hands hath he recompensed me.}

\enubox{21 For I have kept the ways of the LORD, and have not wickedly departed from my God.}

\enubox{22 For all his judgments were before me, and I did not put away his statutes from me.}

\enubox{23 I was also upright before him, and I kept myself from mine iniquity.}

\enubox{24 Therefore hath the LORD recompensed me according to my righteousness, according to the cleanness of my hands in his eyesight.}

\enubox{25 With the merciful thou wilt shew thyself merciful; with an upright man thou wilt shew thyself upright;}

\enubox{26 With the pure thou wilt shew thyself pure; and with the froward thou wilt shew thyself froward.}

\enubox{27 For thou wilt save the afflicted people; but wilt bring down high looks.}

\enubox{28 For thou wilt light my candle: the LORD my God will enlighten my darkness.}

\enubox{29 For by thee I have run through a troop; and by my God have I leaped over a wall.}

\enubox{30 As for God, his way is perfect: the word of the LORD is tried: he is a buckler to all those that trust in him.}

\enubox{31 For who is God save the LORD? or who is a rock save our God?}

\enubox{32 It is God that girdeth me with strength, and maketh my way perfect.}

\enubox{33 He maketh my feet like hinds' feet, and setteth me upon my high places.}

\enubox{34 He teacheth my hands to war, so that a bow of steel is broken by mine arms.}

\enubox{35 Thou hast also given me the shield of thy salvation: and thy right hand hath holden me up, and thy gentleness hath made me great.}

\enubox{36 Thou hast enlarged my steps under me, that my feet did not slip.}

\enubox{37 I have pursued mine enemies, and overtaken them: neither did I turn again till they were consumed.}

\enubox{38 I have wounded them that they were not able to rise: they are fallen under my feet.}

\enubox{39 For thou hast girded me with strength unto the battle: thou hast subdued under me those that rose up against me.}

\enubox{40 Thou hast also given me the necks of mine enemies; that I might destroy them that hate me.}

\enubox{41 They cried, but there was none to save them: even unto the LORD, but he answered them not.}

\enubox{42 Then did I beat them small as the dust before the wind: I did cast them out as the dirt in the streets.}

\enubox{43 Thou hast delivered me from the strivings of the people; and thou hast made me the head of the heathen: a people whom I have not known shall serve me.}

\enubox{44 As soon as they hear of me, they shall obey me: the strangers shall submit themselves unto me.}

\enubox{45 The strangers shall fade away, and be afraid out of their close places.}

\enubox{46 The LORD liveth; and blessed be my rock; and let the God of my salvation be exalted.}

\enubox{47 It is God that avengeth me, and subdueth the people under me.}

\enubox{48 He delivereth me from mine enemies: yea, thou liftest me up above those that rise up against me: thou hast delivered me from the violent man.}

\enubox{49 Therefore will I give thanks unto thee, O LORD, among the heathen, and sing praises unto thy name.}

\enubox{50 Great deliverance giveth he to his king; and sheweth mercy to his anointed, to David, and to his seed for evermore.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 19}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M524x522S1ce00502x490S2e00e477x479 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 The heavens declare the glory of God; and the firmament sheweth his handywork.}

\enubox{2 Day unto day uttereth speech, and night unto night sheweth knowledge.}

\enubox{3 There is no speech nor language, where their voice is not heard.}

\enubox{4 Their line is gone out through all the earth, and their words to the end of the world. In them hath he set a tabernacle for the sun,}

\enubox{5 Which is as a bridegroom coming out of his chamber, and rejoiceth as a strong man to run a race.}

\enubox{6 His going forth is from the end of the heaven, and his circuit unto the ends of it: and there is nothing hid from the heat thereof.}

\enubox{7 The law of the LORD is perfect, converting the soul: the testimony of the LORD is sure, making wise the simple.}

\enubox{8 The statutes of the LORD are right, rejoicing the heart: the commandment of the LORD is pure, enlightening the eyes.}

\enubox{9 The fear of the LORD is clean, enduring for ever: the judgments of the LORD are true and righteous altogether.}

\enubox{10 More to be desired are they than gold, yea, than much fine gold: sweeter also than honey and the honeycomb.}

\enubox{11 Moreover by them is thy servant warned: and in keeping of them there is great reward.}

\enubox{12 Who can understand his errors? cleanse thou me from secret faults.}

\enubox{13 Keep back thy servant also from presumptuous sins; let them not have dominion over me: then shall I be upright, and I shall be innocent from the great transgression.}

\enubox{14 Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart, be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.}

\enubox{\bf Chapter 20}

\end{center}


\enubox{1 The LORD hear thee in the day of trouble; the name of the God of Jacob defend thee;}

\enubox{2 Send thee help from the sanctuary, and strengthen thee out of Zion;}

\enubox{3 Remember all thy offerings, and accept thy burnt sacrifice; Selah.}

\enubox{4 Grant thee according to thine own heart, and fulfil all thy counsel.}

\enubox{5 We will rejoice in thy salvation, and in the name of our God we will set up our banners: the LORD fulfil all thy petitions.}

\enubox{6 Now know I that the LORD saveth his anointed; he will hear him from his holy heaven with the saving strength of his right hand.}

\enubox{7 Some trust in chariots, and some in horses: but we will remember the name of the LORD our God.}

\enubox{8 They are brought down and fallen: but we are risen, and stand upright.}

\enubox{9 Save, LORD: let the king hear us when we call.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 21}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M517x515S1e020494x485S21802484x497 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 The king shall joy in thy strength, O LORD; and in thy salvation how greatly shall he rejoice!}

\enubox{2 Thou hast given him his heart's desire, and hast not withholden the request of his lips. Selah.}

\enubox{3 For thou preventest him with the blessings of goodness: thou settest a crown of pure gold on his head.}

\enubox{4 He asked life of thee, and thou gavest it him, even length of days for ever and ever.}

\enubox{5 His glory is great in thy salvation: honour and majesty hast thou laid upon him.}

\enubox{6 For thou hast made him most blessed for ever: thou hast made him exceeding glad with thy countenance.}

\enubox{7 For the king trusteth in the LORD, and through the mercy of the most High he shall not be moved.}

\enubox{8 Thine hand shall find out all thine enemies: thy right hand shall find out those that hate thee.}

\enubox{9 Thou shalt make them as a fiery oven in the time of thine anger: the LORD shall swallow them up in his wrath, and the fire shall devour them.}

\enubox{10 Their fruit shalt thou destroy from the earth, and their seed from among the children of men.}

\enubox{11 For they intended evil against thee: they imagined a mischievous device, which they are not able to perform.}

\enubox{12 Therefore shalt thou make them turn their back, when thou shalt make ready thine arrows upon thy strings against the face of them.}

\enubox{13 Be thou exalted, LORD, in thine own strength: so will we sing and praise thy power.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 22}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M518x528S10e50485x472S22f04483x514S26606488x501 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 My God, my God, why hast thou forsaken me? why art thou so far from helping me, and from the words of my roaring?}

\enubox{2 O my God, I cry in the day time, but thou hearest not; and in the night season, and am not silent.}

\enubox{3 But thou art holy, O thou that inhabitest the praises of Israel.}

\enubox{4 Our fathers trusted in thee: they trusted, and thou didst deliver them.}

\enubox{5 They cried unto thee, and were delivered: they trusted in thee, and were not confounded.}

\enubox{6 But I am a worm, and no man; a reproach of men, and despised of the people.}

\enubox{7 All they that see me laugh me to scorn: they shoot out the lip, they shake the head, saying,}

\enubox{8 He trusted on the LORD that he would deliver him: let him deliver him, seeing he delighted in him.}

\enubox{9 But thou art he that took me out of the womb: thou didst make me hope when I was upon my mother's breasts.}

\enubox{10 I was cast upon thee from the womb: thou art my God from my mother's belly.}

\enubox{11 Be not far from me; for trouble is near; for there is none to help.}

\enubox{12 Many bulls have compassed me: strong bulls of Bashan have beset me round.}

\enubox{13 They gaped upon me with their mouths, as a ravening and a roaring lion.}

\enubox{14 I am poured out like water, and all my bones are out of joint: my heart is like wax; it is melted in the midst of my bowels.}

\enubox{15 My strength is dried up like a potsherd; and my tongue cleaveth to my jaws; and thou hast brought me into the dust of death.}

\enubox{16 For dogs have compassed me: the assembly of the wicked have inclosed me: they pierced my hands and my feet.}

\enubox{17 I may tell all my bones: they look and stare upon me.}

\enubox{18 They part my garments among them, and cast lots upon my vesture.}

\enubox{19 But be not thou far from me, O LORD: O my strength, haste thee to help me.}

\enubox{20 Deliver my soul from the sword; my darling from the power of the dog.}

\enubox{21 Save me from the lion's mouth: for thou hast heard me from the horns of the unicorns.}

\enubox{22 I will declare thy name unto my brethren: in the midst of the congregation will I praise thee.}

\enubox{23 Ye that fear the LORD, praise him; all ye the seed of Jacob, glorify him; and fear him, all ye the seed of Israel.}

\enubox{24 For he hath not despised nor abhorred the affliction of the afflicted; neither hath he hid his face from him; but when he cried unto him, he heard.}

\enubox{25 My praise shall be of thee in the great congregation: I will pay my vows before them that fear him.}

\enubox{26 The meek shall eat and be satisfied: they shall praise the LORD that seek him: your heart shall live for ever.}

\enubox{27 All the ends of the world shall remember and turn unto the LORD: and all the kindreds of the nations shall worship before thee.}

\enubox{28 For the kingdom is the LORD's: and he is the governor among the nations.}

\enubox{29 All they that be fat upon earth shall eat and worship: all they that go down to the dust shall bow before him: and none can keep alive his own soul.}

\enubox{30 A seed shall serve him; it shall be accounted to the Lord for a generation.}

\enubox{31 They shall come, and shall declare his righteousness unto a people that shall be born, that he hath done this.}

\enubox{1 The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.}

\enubox{2 He maketh me to lie down in green pastures: he leadeth me beside the still waters.}

\enubox{3 He restoreth my soul: he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.}

\enubox{4 Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death, I will fear no evil: for thou art with me; thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.}

\enubox{5 Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies: thou anointest my head with oil; my cup runneth over.}

\enubox{6 Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life: and I will dwell in the house of the LORD for ever.}

\enubox{1 The earth is the LORD's, and the fulness thereof; the world, and they that dwell therein.}

\enubox{2 For he hath founded it upon the seas, and established it upon the floods.}

\enubox{3 Who shall ascend into the hill of the LORD? or who shall stand in his holy place?}

\enubox{4 He that hath clean hands, and a pure heart; who hath not lifted up his soul unto vanity, nor sworn deceitfully.}

\enubox{5 He shall receive the blessing from the LORD, and righteousness from the God of his salvation.}

\enubox{6 This is the generation of them that seek him, that seek thy face, O Jacob. Selah.}

\enubox{7 Lift up your heads, O ye gates; and be ye lift up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.}

\enubox{8 Who is this King of glory? The LORD strong and mighty, the LORD mighty in battle.}

\enubox{9 Lift up your heads, O ye gates; even lift them up, ye everlasting doors; and the King of glory shall come in.}

\enubox{10 Who is this King of glory? The LORD of hosts, he is the King of glory. Selah.}

\enubox{1 Unto thee, O LORD, do I lift up my soul.}

\enubox{2 O my God, I trust in thee: let me not be ashamed, let not mine enemies triumph over me.}

\enubox{3 Yea, let none that wait on thee be ashamed: let them be ashamed which transgress without cause.}

\enubox{4 Shew me thy ways, O LORD; teach me thy paths.}

\enubox{5 Lead me in thy truth, and teach me: for thou art the God of my salvation; on thee do I wait all the day.}

\enubox{6 Remember, O LORD, thy tender mercies and thy lovingkindnesses; for they have been ever of old.}

\enubox{7 Remember not the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions: according to thy mercy remember thou me for thy goodness' sake, O LORD.}

\enubox{8 Good and upright is the LORD: therefore will he teach sinners in the way.}

\enubox{9 The meek will he guide in judgment: and the meek will he teach his way.}

\enubox{10 All the paths of the LORD are mercy and truth unto such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.}

\enubox{11 For thy name's sake, O LORD, pardon mine iniquity; for it is great.}

\enubox{12 What man is he that feareth the LORD? him shall he teach in the way that he shall choose.}

\enubox{13 His soul shall dwell at ease; and his seed shall inherit the earth.}

\enubox{14 The secret of the LORD is with them that fear him; and he will shew them his covenant.}

\enubox{15 Mine eyes are ever toward the LORD; for he shall pluck my feet out of the net.}

\enubox{16 Turn thee unto me, and have mercy upon me; for I am desolate and afflicted.}

\enubox{17 The troubles of my heart are enlarged: O bring thou me out of my distresses.}

\enubox{18 Look upon mine affliction and my pain; and forgive all my sins.}

\enubox{19 Consider mine enemies; for they are many; and they hate me with cruel hatred.}

\enubox{20 O keep my soul, and deliver me: let me not be ashamed; for I put my trust in thee.}

\enubox{21 Let integrity and uprightness preserve me; for I wait on thee.}

\enubox{22 Redeem Israel, O God, out of all his troubles.}

\enubox{1 Judge me, O LORD; for I have walked in mine integrity: I have trusted also in the LORD; therefore I shall not slide.}

\enubox{2 Examine me, O LORD, and prove me; try my reins and my heart.}

\enubox{3 For thy lovingkindness is before mine eyes: and I have walked in thy truth.}

\enubox{4 I have not sat with vain persons, neither will I go in with dissemblers.}

\enubox{5 I have hated the congregation of evil doers; and will not sit with the wicked.}

\enubox{6 I will wash mine hands in innocency: so will I compass thine altar, O LORD:}

\enubox{7 That I may publish with the voice of thanksgiving, and tell of all thy wondrous works.}

\enubox{8 LORD, I have loved the habitation of thy house, and the place where thine honour dwelleth.}

\enubox{9 Gather not my soul with sinners, nor my life with bloody men:}

\enubox{10 In whose hands is mischief, and their right hand is full of bribes.}

\enubox{11 But as for me, I will walk in mine integrity: redeem me, and be merciful unto me.}

\enubox{12 My foot standeth in an even place: in the congregations will I bless the LORD.}

\enubox{1 The LORD is my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear? the LORD is the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?}

\enubox{2 When the wicked, even mine enemies and my foes, came upon me to eat up my flesh, they stumbled and fell.}

\enubox{3 Though an host should encamp against me, my heart shall not fear: though war should rise against me, in this will I be confident.}

\enubox{4 One thing have I desired of the LORD, that will I seek after; that I may dwell in the house of the LORD all the days of my life, to behold the beauty of the LORD, and to enquire in his temple.}

\enubox{5 For in the time of trouble he shall hide me in his pavilion: in the secret of his tabernacle shall he hide me; he shall set me up upon a rock.}

\enubox{6 And now shall mine head be lifted up above mine enemies round about me: therefore will I offer in his tabernacle sacrifices of joy; I will sing, yea, I will sing praises unto the LORD.}

\enubox{7 Hear, O LORD, when I cry with my voice: have mercy also upon me, and answer me.}

\enubox{8 When thou saidst, Seek ye my face; my heart said unto thee, Thy face, LORD, will I seek.}

\enubox{9 Hide not thy face far from me; put not thy servant away in anger: thou hast been my help; leave me not, neither forsake me, O God of my salvation.}

\enubox{10 When my father and my mother forsake me, then the LORD will take me up.}

\enubox{11 Teach me thy way, O LORD, and lead me in a plain path, because of mine enemies.}

\enubox{12 Deliver me not over unto the will of mine enemies: for false witnesses are risen up against me, and such as breathe out cruelty.}

\enubox{13 I had fainted, unless I had believed to see the goodness of the LORD in the land of the living.}

\enubox{14 Wait on the LORD: be of good courage, and he shall strengthen thine heart: wait, I say, on the LORD.}

\enubox{1 Unto thee will I cry, O LORD my rock; be not silent to me: lest, if thou be silent to me, I become like them that go down into the pit.}

\enubox{2 Hear the voice of my supplications, when I cry unto thee, when I lift up my hands toward thy holy oracle.}

\enubox{3 Draw me not away with the wicked, and with the workers of iniquity, which speak peace to their neighbours, but mischief is in their hearts.}

\enubox{4 Give them according to their deeds, and according to the wickedness of their endeavours: give them after the work of their hands; render to them their desert.}

\enubox{5 Because they regard not the works of the LORD, nor the operation of his hands, he shall destroy them, and not build them up.}

\enubox{6 Blessed be the LORD, because he hath heard the voice of my supplications.}

\enubox{7 The LORD is my strength and my shield; my heart trusted in him, and I am helped: therefore my heart greatly rejoiceth; and with my song will I praise him.}

\enubox{8 The LORD is their strength, and he is the saving strength of his anointed.}

\enubox{9 Save thy people, and bless thine inheritance: feed them also, and lift them up for ever.}

\enubox{10 The LORD sitteth upon the flood; yea, the LORD sitteth King for ever.}

\enubox{11 The LORD will give strength unto his people; the LORD will bless his people with peace.}

\enubox{1 I will extol thee, O LORD; for thou hast lifted me up, and hast not made my foes to rejoice over me.}

\enubox{2 O LORD my God, I cried unto thee, and thou hast healed me.}

\enubox{3 O LORD, thou hast brought up my soul from the grave: thou hast kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.}

\enubox{4 Sing unto the LORD, O ye saints of his, and give thanks at the remembrance of his holiness.}

\enubox{5 For his anger endureth but a moment; in his favour is life: weeping may endure for a night, but joy cometh in the morning.}

\enubox{6 And in my prosperity I said, I shall never be moved.}

\enubox{7 LORD, by thy favour thou hast made my mountain to stand strong: thou didst hide thy face, and I was troubled.}

\enubox{8 I cried to thee, O LORD; and unto the LORD I made supplication.}

\enubox{9 What profit is there in my blood, when I go down to the pit? Shall the dust praise thee? shall it declare thy truth?}

\enubox{10 Hear, O LORD, and have mercy upon me: LORD, be thou my helper.}

\enubox{11 Thou hast turned for me my mourning into dancing: thou hast put off my sackcloth, and girded me with gladness;}

\enubox{12 To the end that my glory may sing praise to thee, and not be silent. O LORD my God, I will give thanks unto thee for ever.}

\enubox{4 Pull me out of the net that they have laid privily for me: for thou art my strength.}

\enubox{6 I have hated them that regard lying vanities: but I trust in the LORD.}

\enubox{7 I will be glad and rejoice in thy mercy: for thou hast considered my trouble; thou hast known my soul in adversities;}

\enubox{8 And hast not shut me up into the hand of the enemy: thou hast set my feet in a large room.}

\enubox{9 Have mercy upon me, O LORD, for I am in trouble: mine eye is consumed with grief, yea, my soul and my belly.}

\enubox{10 For my life is spent with grief, and my years with sighing: my strength faileth because of mine iniquity, and my bones are consumed.}

\enubox{11 I was a reproach among all mine enemies, but especially among my neighbours, and a fear to mine acquaintance: they that did see me without fled from me.}

\enubox{12 I am forgotten as a dead man out of mind: I am like a broken vessel.}

\enubox{13 For I have heard the slander of many: fear was on every side: while they took counsel together against me, they devised to take away my life.}

\enubox{14 But I trusted in thee, O LORD: I said, Thou art my God.}

\enubox{15 My times are in thy hand: deliver me from the hand of mine enemies, and from them that persecute me.}

\enubox{16 Make thy face to shine upon thy servant: save me for thy mercies' sake.}

\enubox{17 Let me not be ashamed, O LORD; for I have called upon thee: let the wicked be ashamed, and let them be silent in the grave.}

\enubox{18 Let the lying lips be put to silence; which speak grievous things proudly and contemptuously against the righteous.}

\enubox{19 Oh how great is thy goodness, which thou hast laid up for them that fear thee; which thou hast wrought for them that trust in thee before the sons of men!}

\enubox{20 Thou shalt hide them in the secret of thy presence from the pride of man: thou shalt keep them secretly in a pavilion from the strife of tongues.}

\enubox{21 Blessed be the LORD: for he hath shewed me his marvellous kindness in a strong city.}

\enubox{22 For I said in my haste, I am cut off from before thine eyes: nevertheless thou heardest the voice of my supplications when I cried unto thee.}

\enubox{23 O love the LORD, all ye his saints: for the LORD preserveth the faithful, and plentifully rewardeth the proud doer.}

\enubox{24 Be of good courage, and he shall strengthen your heart, all ye that hope in the LORD.}

\enubox{1 Blessed is he whose transgression is forgiven, whose sin is covered.}

\enubox{2 Blessed is the man unto whom the LORD imputeth not iniquity, and in whose spirit there is no guile.}

\enubox{3 When I kept silence, my bones waxed old through my roaring all the day long.}

\enubox{4 For day and night thy hand was heavy upon me: my moisture is turned into the drought of summer. Selah.}

\enubox{5 I acknowledge my sin unto thee, and mine iniquity have I not hid. I said, I will confess my transgressions unto the LORD; and thou forgavest the iniquity of my sin. Selah.}

\enubox{6 For this shall every one that is godly pray unto thee in a time when thou mayest be found: surely in the floods of great waters they shall not come nigh unto him.}

\enubox{7 Thou art my hiding place; thou shalt preserve me from trouble; thou shalt compass me about with songs of deliverance. Selah.}

\enubox{8 I will instruct thee and teach thee in the way which thou shalt go: I will guide thee with mine eye.}

\enubox{9 Be ye not as the horse, or as the mule, which have no understanding: whose mouth must be held in with bit and bridle, lest they come near unto thee.}

\enubox{10 Many sorrows shall be to the wicked: but he that trusteth in the LORD, mercy shall compass him about.}

\enubox{11 Be glad in the LORD, and rejoice, ye righteous: and shout for joy, all ye that are upright in heart.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 33}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Rejoice in the LORD, O ye righteous: for praise is comely for the upright.}

\enubox{2 Praise the LORD with harp: sing unto him with the psaltery and an instrument of ten strings.}

\enubox{3 Sing unto him a new song; play skilfully with a loud noise.}

\enubox{4 For the word of the LORD is right; and all his works are done in truth.}

\enubox{5 He loveth righteousness and judgment: the earth is full of the goodness of the LORD.}

\enubox{6 By the word of the LORD were the heavens made; and all the host of them by the breath of his mouth.}

\enubox{7 He gathereth the waters of the sea together as an heap: he layeth up the depth in storehouses.}

\enubox{8 Let all the earth fear the LORD: let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.}

\enubox{9 For he spake, and it was done; he commanded, and it stood fast.}

\enubox{10 The LORD bringeth the counsel of the heathen to nought: he maketh the devices of the people of none effect.}

\enubox{11 The counsel of the LORD standeth for ever, the thoughts of his heart to all generations.}

\enubox{12 Blessed is the nation whose God is the LORD; and the people whom he hath chosen for his own inheritance.}

\enubox{13 The LORD looketh from heaven; he beholdeth all the sons of men.}

\enubox{14 From the place of his habitation he looketh upon all the inhabitants of the earth.}

\enubox{15 He fashioneth their hearts alike; he considereth all their works.}

\enubox{16 There is no king saved by the multitude of an host: a mighty man is not delivered by much strength.}

\enubox{17 An horse is a vain thing for safety: neither shall he deliver any by his great strength.}

\enubox{18 Behold, the eye of the LORD is upon them that fear him, upon them that hope in his mercy;}

\enubox{19 To deliver their soul from death, and to keep them alive in famine.}

\enubox{20 Our soul waiteth for the LORD: he is our help and our shield.}

\enubox{21 For our heart shall rejoice in him, because we have trusted in his holy name.}

\enubox{22 Let thy mercy, O LORD, be upon us, according as we hope in thee.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 34}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x516S14400489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I will bless the LORD at all times: his praise shall continually be in my mouth.}

\enubox{2 My soul shall make her boast in the LORD: the humble shall hear thereof, and be glad.}

\enubox{3 O magnify the LORD with me, and let us exalt his name together.}

\enubox{4 I sought the LORD, and he heard me, and delivered me from all my fears.}

\enubox{5 They looked unto him, and were lightened: and their faces were not ashamed.}

\enubox{6 This poor man cried, and the LORD heard him, and saved him out of all his troubles.}

\enubox{7 The angel of the LORD encampeth round about them that fear him, and delivereth them.}

\enubox{8 O taste and see that the LORD is good: blessed is the man that trusteth in him.}

\enubox{9 O fear the LORD, ye his saints: for there is no want to them that fear him.}

\enubox{10 The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger: but they that seek the LORD shall not want any good thing.}

\enubox{11 Come, ye children, hearken unto me: I will teach you the fear of the LORD.}

\enubox{12 What man is he that desireth life, and loveth many days, that he may see good?}

\enubox{13 Keep thy tongue from evil, and thy lips from speaking guile.}

\enubox{14 Depart from evil, and do good; seek peace, and pursue it.}

\enubox{15 The eyes of the LORD are upon the righteous, and his ears are open unto their cry.}

\enubox{16 The face of the LORD is against them that do evil, to cut off the remembrance of them from the earth.}

\enubox{17 The righteous cry, and the LORD heareth, and delivereth them out of all their troubles.}

\enubox{18 The LORD is nigh unto them that are of a broken heart; and saveth such as be of a contrite spirit.}

\enubox{19 Many are the afflictions of the righteous: but the LORD delivereth him out of them all.}

\enubox{20 He keepeth all his bones: not one of them is broken.}

\enubox{21 Evil shall slay the wicked: and they that hate the righteous shall be desolate.}

\enubox{22 The LORD redeemeth the soul of his servants: and none of them that trust in him shall be desolate.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 35}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Plead my cause, O LORD, with them that strive with me: fight against them that fight against me.}

\enubox{2 Take hold of shield and buckler, and stand up for mine help.}

\enubox{3 Draw out also the spear, and stop the way against them that persecute me: say unto my soul, I am thy salvation.}

\enubox{4 Let them be confounded and put to shame that seek after my soul: let them be turned back and brought to confusion that devise my hurt.}

\enubox{5 Let them be as chaff before the wind: and let the angel of the LORD chase them.}

\enubox{6 Let their way be dark and slippery: and let the angel of the LORD persecute them.}

\enubox{7 For without cause have they hid for me their net in a pit, which without cause they have digged for my soul.}

\enubox{8 Let destruction come upon him at unawares; and let his net that he hath hid catch himself: into that very destruction let him fall.}

\enubox{9 And my soul shall be joyful in the LORD: it shall rejoice in his salvation.}

\enubox{10 All my bones shall say, LORD, who is like unto thee, which deliverest the poor from him that is too strong for him, yea, the poor and the needy from him that spoileth him?}

\enubox{11 False witnesses did rise up; they laid to my charge things that I knew not.}

\enubox{12 They rewarded me evil for good to the spoiling of my soul.}

\enubox{13 But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth: I humbled my soul with fasting; and my prayer returned into mine own bosom.}

\enubox{14 I behaved myself as though he had been my friend or brother: I bowed down heavily, as one that mourneth for his mother.}

\enubox{15 But in mine adversity they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together: yea, the abjects gathered themselves together against me, and I knew it not; they did tear me, and ceased not:}

\enubox{16 With hypocritical mockers in feasts, they gnashed upon me with their teeth.}

\enubox{17 Lord, how long wilt thou look on? rescue my soul from their destructions, my darling from the lions.}

\enubox{18 I will give thee thanks in the great congregation: I will praise thee among much people.}

\enubox{19 Let not them that are mine enemies wrongfully rejoice over me: neither let them wink with the eye that hate me without a cause.}

\enubox{20 For they speak not peace: but they devise deceitful matters against them that are quiet in the land.}

\enubox{21 Yea, they opened their mouth wide against me, and said, Aha, aha, our eye hath seen it.}

\enubox{22 This thou hast seen, O LORD: keep not silence: O Lord, be not far from me.}

\enubox{23 Stir up thyself, and awake to my judgment, even unto my cause, my God and my Lord.}

\enubox{24 Judge me, O LORD my God, according to thy righteousness; and let them not rejoice over me.}

\enubox{25 Let them not say in their hearts, Ah, so would we have it: let them not say, We have swallowed him up.}

\enubox{26 Let them be ashamed and brought to confusion together that rejoice at mine hurt: let them be clothed with shame and dishonour that magnify themselves against me.}

\enubox{27 Let them shout for joy, and be glad, that favour my righteous cause: yea, let them say continually, Let the LORD be magnified, which hath pleasure in the prosperity of his servant.}

\enubox{28 And my tongue shall speak of thy righteousness and of thy praise all the day long.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 36}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M509x515S18720491x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 The transgression of the wicked saith within my heart, that there is no fear of God before his eyes.}

\enubox{2 For he flattereth himself in his own eyes, until his iniquity be found to be hateful.}

\enubox{3 The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit: he hath left off to be wise, and to do good.}

\enubox{4 He deviseth mischief upon his bed; he setteth himself in a way that is not good; he abhorreth not evil.}

\enubox{5 Thy mercy, O LORD, is in the heavens; and thy faithfulness reacheth unto the clouds.}

\enubox{6 Thy righteousness is like the great mountains; thy judgments are a great deep: O LORD, thou preservest man and beast.}

\enubox{7 How excellent is thy lovingkindness, O God! therefore the children of men put their trust under the shadow of thy wings.}

\enubox{8 They shall be abundantly satisfied with the fatness of thy house; and thou shalt make them drink of the river of thy pleasures.}

\enubox{9 For with thee is the fountain of life: in thy light shall we see light.}

\enubox{10 O continue thy lovingkindness unto them that know thee; and thy righteousness to the upright in heart.}

\enubox{11 Let not the foot of pride come against me, and let not the hand of the wicked remove me.}

\enubox{12 There are the workers of iniquity fallen: they are cast down, and shall not be able to rise.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 37}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x514S1a520490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Fret not thyself because of evildoers, neither be thou envious against the workers of iniquity.}

\enubox{2 For they shall soon be cut down like the grass, and wither as the green herb.}

\enubox{3 Trust in the LORD, and do good; so shalt thou dwell in the land, and verily thou shalt be fed.}

\enubox{4 Delight thyself also in the LORD: and he shall give thee the desires of thine heart.}

\enubox{5 Commit thy way unto the LORD; trust also in him; and he shall bring it to pass.}

\enubox{6 And he shall bring forth thy righteousness as the light, and thy judgment as the noonday.}

\enubox{7 Rest in the LORD, and wait patiently for him: fret not thyself because of him who prospereth in his way, because of the man who bringeth wicked devices to pass.}

\enubox{8 Cease from anger, and forsake wrath: fret not thyself in any wise to do evil.}

\enubox{9 For evildoers shall be cut off: but those that wait upon the LORD, they shall inherit the earth.}

\enubox{10 For yet a little while, and the wicked shall not be: yea, thou shalt diligently consider his place, and it shall not be.}

\enubox{11 But the meek shall inherit the earth; and shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.}

\enubox{12 The wicked plotteth against the just, and gnasheth upon him with his teeth.}

\enubox{13 The LORD shall laugh at him: for he seeth that his day is coming.}

\enubox{14 The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow, to cast down the poor and needy, and to slay such as be of upright conversation.}

\enubox{15 Their sword shall enter into their own heart, and their bows shall be broken.}

\enubox{16 A little that a righteous man hath is better than the riches of many wicked.}

\enubox{17 For the arms of the wicked shall be broken: but the LORD upholdeth the righteous.}

\enubox{18 The LORD knoweth the days of the upright: and their inheritance shall be for ever.}

\enubox{19 They shall not be ashamed in the evil time: and in the days of famine they shall be satisfied.}

\enubox{20 But the wicked shall perish, and the enemies of the LORD shall be as the fat of lambs: they shall consume; into smoke shall they consume away.}

\enubox{21 The wicked borroweth, and payeth not again: but the righteous sheweth mercy, and giveth.}

\enubox{22 For such as be blessed of him shall inherit the earth; and they that be cursed of him shall be cut off.}

\enubox{23 The steps of a good man are ordered by the LORD: and he delighteth in his way.}

\enubox{24 Though he fall, he shall not be utterly cast down: for the LORD upholdeth him with his hand.}

\enubox{25 I have been young, and now am old; yet have I not seen the righteous forsaken, nor his seed begging bread.}

\enubox{26 He is ever merciful, and lendeth; and his seed is blessed.}

\enubox{27 Depart from evil, and do good; and dwell for evermore.}

\enubox{28 For the LORD loveth judgment, and forsaketh not his saints; they are preserved for ever: but the seed of the wicked shall be cut off.}

\enubox{29 The righteous shall inherit the land, and dwell therein for ever.}

\enubox{30 The mouth of the righteous speaketh wisdom, and his tongue talketh of judgment.}

\enubox{31 The law of his God is in his heart; none of his steps shall slide.}

\enubox{32 The wicked watcheth the righteous, and seeketh to slay him.}

\enubox{33 The LORD will not leave him in his hand, nor condemn him when he is judged.}

\enubox{34 Wait on the LORD, and keep his way, and he shall exalt thee to inherit the land: when the wicked are cut off, thou shalt see it.}

\enubox{35 I have seen the wicked in great power, and spreading himself like a green bay tree.}

\enubox{36 Yet he passed away, and, lo, he was not: yea, I sought him, but he could not be found.}

\enubox{37 Mark the perfect man, and behold the upright: for the end of that man is peace.}

\enubox{38 But the transgressors shall be destroyed together: the end of the wicked shall be cut off.}

\enubox{39 But the salvation of the righteous is of the LORD: he is their strength in the time of trouble.}

\enubox{40 And the LORD shall help them, and deliver them: he shall deliver them from the wicked, and save them, because they trust in him.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 38}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x514S1bb20490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O lord, rebuke me not in thy wrath: neither chasten me in thy hot displeasure.}

\enubox{2 For thine arrows stick fast in me, and thy hand presseth me sore.}

\enubox{3 There is no soundness in my flesh because of thine anger; neither is there any rest in my bones because of my sin.}

\enubox{4 For mine iniquities are gone over mine head: as an heavy burden they are too heavy for me.}

\enubox{5 My wounds stink and are corrupt because of my foolishness.}

\enubox{6 I am troubled; I am bowed down greatly; I go mourning all the day long.}

\enubox{7 For my loins are filled with a loathsome disease: and there is no soundness in my flesh.}

\enubox{8 I am feeble and sore broken: I have roared by reason of the disquietness of my heart.}

\enubox{9 Lord, all my desire is before thee; and my groaning is not hid from thee.}

\enubox{10 My heart panteth, my strength faileth me: as for the light of mine eyes, it also is gone from me.}

\enubox{11 My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my sore; and my kinsmen stand afar off.}

\enubox{12 They also that seek after my life lay snares for me: and they that seek my hurt speak mischievous things, and imagine deceits all the day long.}

\enubox{13 But I, as a deaf man, heard not; and I was as a dumb man that openeth not his mouth.}

\enubox{14 Thus I was as a man that heareth not, and in whose mouth are no reproofs.}

\enubox{15 For in thee, O LORD, do I hope: thou wilt hear, O Lord my God.}

\enubox{16 For I said, Hear me, lest otherwise they should rejoice over me: when my foot slippeth, they magnify themselves against me.}

\enubox{17 For I am ready to halt, and my sorrow is continually before me.}

\enubox{18 For I will declare mine iniquity; I will be sorry for my sin.}

\enubox{19 But mine enemies are lively, and they are strong: and they that hate me wrongfully are multiplied.}

\enubox{20 They also that render evil for good are mine adversaries; because I follow the thing that good is.}

\enubox{21 Forsake me not, O LORD: O my God, be not far from me.}

\enubox{22 Make haste to help me, O Lord my salvation.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 39}

\enubox{1 I said, I will take heed to my ways, that I sin not with my tongue: I will keep my mouth with a bridle, while the wicked is before me.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 40}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M508x508S17610492x492 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I waited patiently for the LORD; and he inclined unto me, and heard my cry.}

\enubox{2 He brought me up also out of an horrible pit, out of the miry clay, and set my feet upon a rock, and established my goings.}

\enubox{3 And he hath put a new song in my mouth, even praise unto our God: many shall see it, and fear, and shall trust in the LORD.}

\enubox{4 Blessed is that man that maketh the LORD his trust, and respecteth not the proud, nor such as turn aside to lies.}

\enubox{5 Many, O LORD my God, are thy wonderful works which thou hast done, and thy thoughts which are to us-ward: they cannot be reckoned up in order unto thee: if I would declare and speak of them, they are more than can be numbered.}

\enubox{6 Sacrifice and offering thou didst not desire; mine ears hast thou opened: burnt offering and sin offering hast thou not required.}

\enubox{7 Then said I, Lo, I come: in the volume of the book it is written of me,}

\enubox{8 I delight to do thy will, O my God: yea, thy law is within my heart.}

\enubox{9 I have preached righteousness in the great congregation: lo, I have not refrained my lips, O LORD, thou knowest.}

\enubox{10 I have not hid thy righteousness within my heart; I have declared thy faithfulness and thy salvation: I have not concealed thy lovingkindness and thy truth from the great congregation.}

\enubox{11 Withhold not thou thy tender mercies from me, O LORD: let thy lovingkindness and thy truth continually preserve me.}

\enubox{12 For innumerable evils have compassed me about: mine iniquities have taken hold upon me, so that I am not able to look up; they are more than the hairs of mine head: therefore my heart faileth me.}

\enubox{13 Be pleased, O LORD, to deliver me: O LORD, make haste to help me.}

\enubox{14 Let them be ashamed and confounded together that seek after my soul to destroy it; let them be driven backward and put to shame that wish me evil.}

\enubox{15 Let them be desolate for a reward of their shame that say unto me, Aha, aha.}

\enubox{16 Let all those that seek thee rejoice and be glad in thee: let such as love thy salvation say continually, The LORD be magnified.}

\enubox{17 But I am poor and needy; yet the Lord thinketh upon me: thou art my help and my deliverer; make no tarrying, O my God.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 41}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M508x515S10000493x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Blessed is he that considereth the poor: the LORD will deliver him in time of trouble.}

\enubox{2 The LORD will preserve him, and keep him alive; and he shall be blessed upon the earth: and thou wilt not deliver him unto the will of his enemies.}

\enubox{3 The LORD will strengthen him upon the bed of languishing: thou wilt make all his bed in his sickness.}

\enubox{4 I said, LORD, be merciful unto me: heal my soul; for I have sinned against thee.}

\enubox{5 Mine enemies speak evil of me, When shall he die, and his name perish?}

\enubox{6 And if he come to see me, he speaketh vanity: his heart gathereth iniquity to itself; when he goeth abroad, he telleth it.}

\enubox{7 All that hate me whisper together against me: against me do they devise my hurt.}

\enubox{8 An evil disease, say they, cleaveth fast unto him: and now that he lieth he shall rise up no more.}

\enubox{9 Yea, mine own familiar friend, in whom I trusted, which did eat of my bread, hath lifted up his heel against me.}

\enubox{10 But thou, O LORD, be merciful unto me, and raise me up, that I may requite them.}

\enubox{11 By this I know that thou favourest me, because mine enemy doth not triumph over me.}

\enubox{12 And as for me, thou upholdest me in mine integrity, and settest me before thy face for ever.}

\enubox{13 Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting, and to everlasting. Amen, and Amen.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 42}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M508x515S10e00493x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 As the hart panteth after the water brooks, so panteth my soul after thee, O God.}

\enubox{2 My soul thirsteth for God, for the living God: when shall I come and appear before God?}

\enubox{3 My tears have been my meat day and night, while they continually say unto me, Where is thy God?}

\enubox{4 When I remember these things, I pour out my soul in me: for I had gone with the multitude, I went with them to the house of God, with the voice of joy and praise, with a multitude that kept holyday.}

\enubox{5 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted in me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him for the help of his countenance.}

\enubox{6 O my God, my soul is cast down within me: therefore will I remember thee from the land of Jordan, and of the Hermonites, from the hill Mizar.}

\enubox{7 Deep calleth unto deep at the noise of thy waterspouts: all thy waves and thy billows are gone over me.}

\enubox{8 Yet the LORD will command his lovingkindness in the day time, and in the night his song shall be with me, and my prayer unto the God of my life.}

\enubox{9 I will say unto God my rock, Why hast thou forgotten me? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?}

\enubox{10 As with a sword in my bones, mine enemies reproach me; while they say daily unto me, Where is thy God?}

\enubox{11 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope thou in God: for I shall yet praise him, who is the health of my countenance, and my God.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 43}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Judge me, O God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation: O deliver me from the deceitful and unjust man.}

\enubox{2 For thou art the God of my strength: why dost thou cast me off? why go I mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?}

\enubox{3 O send out thy light and thy truth: let them lead me; let them bring me unto thy holy hill, and to thy tabernacles.}

\enubox{4 Then will I go unto the altar of God, unto God my exceeding joy: yea, upon the harp will I praise thee, O God my God.}

\enubox{5 Why art thou cast down, O my soul? and why art thou disquieted within me? hope in God: for I shall yet praise him, who is the health of my countenance, and my God.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 44}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M511x516S14400489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 We have heard with our ears, O God, our fathers have told us, what work thou didst in their days, in the times of old.}

\enubox{2 How thou didst drive out the heathen with thy hand, and plantedst them; how thou didst afflict the people, and cast them out.}

\enubox{3 For they got not the land in possession by their own sword, neither did their own arm save them: but thy right hand, and thine arm, and the light of thy countenance, because thou hadst a favour unto them.}

\enubox{4 Thou art my King, O God: command deliverances for Jacob.}

\enubox{5 Through thee will we push down our enemies: through thy name will we tread them under that rise up against us.}

\enubox{6 For I will not trust in my bow, neither shall my sword save me.}

\enubox{7 But thou hast saved us from our enemies, and hast put them to shame that hated us.}

\enubox{8 In God we boast all the day long, and praise thy name for ever. Selah.}

\enubox{9 But thou hast cast off, and put us to shame; and goest not forth with our armies.}

\enubox{10 Thou makest us to turn back from the enemy: and they which hate us spoil for themselves.}

\enubox{11 Thou hast given us like sheep appointed for meat; and hast scattered us among the heathen.}

\enubox{12 Thou sellest thy people for nought, and dost not increase thy wealth by their price.}

\enubox{13 Thou makest us a reproach to our neighbours, a scorn and a derision to them that are round about us.}

\enubox{14 Thou makest us a byword among the heathen, a shaking of the head among the people.}

\enubox{15 My confusion is continually before me, and the shame of my face hath covered me,}

\enubox{16 For the voice of him that reproacheth and blasphemeth; by reason of the enemy and avenger.}

\enubox{17 All this is come upon us; yet have we not forgotten thee, neither have we dealt falsely in thy covenant.}

\enubox{18 Our heart is not turned back, neither have our steps declined from thy way;}

\enubox{19 Though thou hast sore broken us in the place of dragons, and covered us with the shadow of death.}

\enubox{20 If we have forgotten the name of our God, or stretched out our hands to a strange god;}

\enubox{21 Shall not God search this out? for he knoweth the secrets of the heart.}

\enubox{22 Yea, for thy sake are we killed all the day long; we are counted as sheep for the slaughter.}

\enubox{23 Awake, why sleepest thou, O Lord? arise, cast us not off for ever.}

\enubox{24 Wherefore hidest thou thy face, and forgettest our affliction and our oppression?}

\enubox{25 For our soul is bowed down to the dust: our belly cleaveth unto the earth.}

\enubox{26 Arise for our help, and redeem us for thy mercies' sake.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 45}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 My heart is inditing a good matter: I speak of the things which I have made touching the king: my tongue is the pen of a ready writer.}

\enubox{2 Thou art fairer than the children of men: grace is poured into thy lips: therefore God hath blessed thee for ever.}

\enubox{3 Gird thy sword upon thy thigh, O most mighty, with thy glory and thy majesty.}

\enubox{4 And in thy majesty ride prosperously because of truth and meekness and righteousness; and thy right hand shall teach thee terrible things.}

\enubox{5 Thine arrows are sharp in the heart of the king's enemies; whereby the people fall under thee.}

\enubox{6 Thy throne, O God, is for ever and ever: the sceptre of thy kingdom is a right sceptre.}

\enubox{7 Thou lovest righteousness, and hatest wickedness: therefore God, thy God, hath anointed thee with the oil of gladness above thy fellows.}

\enubox{8 All thy garments smell of myrrh, and aloes, and cassia, out of the ivory palaces, whereby they have made thee glad.}

\enubox{9 Kings' daughters were among thy honourable women: upon thy right hand did stand the queen in gold of Ophir.}

\enubox{10 Hearken, O daughter, and consider, and incline thine ear; forget also thine own people, and thy father's house;}

\enubox{11 So shall the king greatly desire thy beauty: for he is thy Lord; and worship thou him.}

\enubox{12 And the daughter of Tyre shall be there with a gift; even the rich among the people shall intreat thy favour.}

\enubox{13 The king's daughter is all glorious within: her clothing is of wrought gold.}

\enubox{14 She shall be brought unto the king in raiment of needlework: the virgins her companions that follow her shall be brought unto thee.}

\enubox{15 With gladness and rejoicing shall they be brought: they shall enter into the king's palace.}

\enubox{16 Instead of thy fathers shall be thy children, whom thou mayest make princes in all the earth.}

\enubox{17 I will make thy name to be remembered in all generations: therefore shall the people praise thee for ever and ever.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 46}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M509x515S18720491x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 God is our refuge and strength, a very present help in trouble.}

\enubox{2 Therefore will not we fear, though the earth be removed, and though the mountains be carried into the midst of the sea;}

\enubox{3 Though the waters thereof roar and be troubled, though the mountains shake with the swelling thereof. Selah.}

\enubox{4 There is a river, the streams whereof shall make glad the city of God, the holy place of the tabernacles of the most High.}

\enubox{5 God is in the midst of her; she shall not be moved: God shall help her, and that right early.}

\enubox{6 The heathen raged, the kingdoms were moved: he uttered his voice, the earth melted.}

\enubox{7 The LORD of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.}

\enubox{8 Come, behold the works of the LORD, what desolations he hath made in the earth.}

\enubox{9 He maketh wars to cease unto the end of the earth; he breaketh the bow, and cutteth the spear in sunder; he burneth the chariot in the fire.}

\enubox{10 Be still, and know that I am God: I will be exalted among the heathen, I will be exalted in the earth.}

\enubox{11 The LORD of hosts is with us; the God of Jacob is our refuge. Selah.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 47}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M511x514S1a520490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O clap your hands, all ye people; shout unto God with the voice of triumph.}

\enubox{2 For the LORD most high is terrible; he is a great King over all the earth.}

\enubox{3 He shall subdue the people under us, and the nations under our feet.}

\enubox{4 He shall choose our inheritance for us, the excellency of Jacob whom he loved. Selah.}

\enubox{5 God is gone up with a shout, the LORD with the sound of a trumpet.}

\enubox{6 Sing praises to God, sing praises: sing praises unto our King, sing praises.}

\enubox{7 For God is the King of all the earth: sing ye praises with understanding.}

\enubox{8 God reigneth over the heathen: God sitteth upon the throne of his holiness.}

\enubox{9 The princes of the people are gathered together, even the people of the God of Abraham: for the shields of the earth belong unto God: he is greatly exalted.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 48}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M511x516S14400489x485 M511x514S1bb20490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised in the city of our God, in the mountain of his holiness.}

\enubox{2 Beautiful for situation, the joy of the whole earth, is mount Zion, on the sides of the north, the city of the great King.}

\enubox{3 God is known in her palaces for a refuge.}

\enubox{4 For, lo, the kings were assembled, they passed by together.}

\enubox{5 They saw it, and so they marvelled; they were troubled, and hasted away.}

\enubox{6 Fear took hold upon them there, and pain, as of a woman in travail.}

\enubox{7 Thou breakest the ships of Tarshish with an east wind.}

\enubox{8 As we have heard, so have we seen in the city of the LORD of hosts, in the city of our God: God will establish it for ever. Selah.}

\enubox{9 We have thought of thy lovingkindness, O God, in the midst of thy temple.}

\enubox{10 According to thy name, O God, so is thy praise unto the ends of the earth: thy right hand is full of righteousness.}

\enubox{11 Let mount Zion rejoice, let the daughters of Judah be glad, because of thy judgments.}

\enubox{12 Walk about Zion, and go round about her: tell the towers thereof.}

\enubox{13 Mark ye well her bulwarks, consider her palaces; that ye may tell it to the generation following.}

\enubox{14 For this God is our God for ever and ever: he will be our guide even unto death.}
