\enubox{1 Bless the LORD, O my soul: and all that is within me, bless his holy name.}

\enubox{2 Bless the LORD, O my soul, and forget not all his benefits:}

\enubox{3 Who forgiveth all thine iniquities; who healeth all thy diseases;}

\enubox{4 Who redeemeth thy life from destruction; who crowneth thee with lovingkindness and tender mercies;}

\enubox{5 Who satisfieth thy mouth with good things; so that thy youth is renewed like the eagle's.}

\enubox{6 The LORD executeth righteousness and judgment for all that are oppressed.}

\enubox{7 He made known his ways unto Moses, his acts unto the children of Israel.}

\enubox{8 The LORD is merciful and gracious, slow to anger, and plenteous in mercy.}

\enubox{9 He will not always chide: neither will he keep his anger for ever.}

\enubox{10 He hath not dealt with us after our sins; nor rewarded us according to our iniquities.}

\enubox{11 For as the heaven is high above the earth, so great is his mercy toward them that fear him.}

\enubox{12 As far as the east is from the west, so far hath he removed our transgressions from us.}

\enubox{13 Like as a father pitieth his children, so the LORD pitieth them that fear him.}

\enubox{14 For he knoweth our frame; he remembereth that we are dust.}

\enubox{15 As for man, his days are as grass: as a flower of the field, so he flourisheth.}

\enubox{16 For the wind passeth over it, and it is gone; and the place thereof shall know it no more.}

\enubox{17 But the mercy of the LORD is from everlasting to everlasting upon them that fear him, and his righteousness unto children's children;}

\enubox{18 To such as keep his covenant, and to those that remember his commandments to do them.}

\enubox{19 The LORD hath prepared his throne in the heavens; and his kingdom ruleth over all.}

\enubox{20 Bless the LORD, ye his angels, that excel in strength, that do his commandments, hearkening unto the voice of his word.}

\enubox{21 Bless ye the LORD, all ye his hosts; ye ministers of his, that do his pleasure.}

\enubox{22 Bless the LORD, all his works in all places of his dominion: bless the LORD, O my soul.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 104}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Bless the LORD, O my soul. O LORD my God, thou art very great; thou art clothed with honour and majesty.}

\enubox{2 Who coverest thyself with light as with a garment: who stretchest out the heavens like a curtain:}

\enubox{3 Who layeth the beams of his chambers in the waters: who maketh the clouds his chariot: who walketh upon the wings of the wind:}

\enubox{4 Who maketh his angels spirits; his ministers a flaming fire:}

\enubox{5 Who laid the foundations of the earth, that it should not be removed for ever.}

\enubox{6 Thou coveredst it with the deep as with a garment: the waters stood above the mountains.}

\enubox{7 At thy rebuke they fled; at the voice of thy thunder they hasted away.}

\enubox{8 They go up by the mountains; they go down by the valleys unto the place which thou hast founded for them.}

\enubox{9 Thou hast set a bound that they may not pass over; that they turn not again to cover the earth.}

\enubox{10 He sendeth the springs into the valleys, which run among the hills.}

\enubox{11 They give drink to every beast of the field: the wild asses quench their thirst.}

\enubox{12 By them shall the fowls of the heaven have their habitation, which sing among the branches.}

\enubox{13 He watereth the hills from his chambers: the earth is satisfied with the fruit of thy works.}

\enubox{14 He causeth the grass to grow for the cattle, and herb for the service of man: that he may bring forth food out of the earth;}

\enubox{15 And wine that maketh glad the heart of man, and oil to make his face to shine, and bread which strengtheneth man's heart.}

\enubox{16 The trees of the LORD are full of sap; the cedars of Lebanon, which he hath planted;}

\enubox{17 Where the birds make their nests: as for the stork, the fir trees are her house.}

\enubox{18 The high hills are a refuge for the wild goats; and the rocks for the conies.}

\enubox{19 He appointed the moon for seasons: the sun knoweth his going down.}

\enubox{20 Thou makest darkness, and it is night: wherein all the beasts of the forest do creep forth.}

\enubox{21 The young lions roar after their prey, and seek their meat from God.}

\enubox{22 The sun ariseth, they gather themselves together, and lay them down in their dens.}

\enubox{23 Man goeth forth unto his work and to his labour until the evening.}

\enubox{24 O LORD, how manifold are thy works! in wisdom hast thou made them all: the earth is full of thy riches.}

\enubox{25 So is this great and wide sea, wherein are things creeping innumerable, both small and great beasts.}

\enubox{26 There go the ships: there is that leviathan, whom thou hast made to play therein.}

\enubox{27 These wait all upon thee; that thou mayest give them their meat in due season.}

\enubox{28 That thou givest them they gather: thou openest thine hand, they are filled with good.}

\enubox{29 Thou hidest thy face, they are troubled: thou takest away their breath, they die, and return to their dust.}

\enubox{30 Thou sendest forth thy spirit, they are created: and thou renewest the face of the earth.}

\enubox{31 The glory of the LORD shall endure for ever: the LORD shall rejoice in his works.}

\enubox{32 He looketh on the earth, and it trembleth: he toucheth the hills, and they smoke.}

\enubox{33 I will sing unto the LORD as long as I live: I will sing praise to my God while I have my being.}

\enubox{34 My meditation of him shall be sweet: I will be glad in the LORD.}

\enubox{35 Let the sinners be consumed out of the earth, and let the wicked be no more. Bless thou the LORD, O my soul. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 105}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O give thanks unto the LORD; call upon his name: make known his deeds among the people.}

\enubox{2 Sing unto him, sing psalms unto him: talk ye of all his wondrous works.}

\enubox{3 Glory ye in his holy name: let the heart of them rejoice that seek the LORD.}

\enubox{4 Seek the LORD, and his strength: seek his face evermore.}

\enubox{5 Remember his marvellous works that he hath done; his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth;}

\enubox{6 O ye seed of Abraham his servant, ye children of Jacob his chosen.}

\enubox{7 He is the LORD our God: his judgments are in all the earth.}

\enubox{8 He hath remembered his covenant for ever, the word which he commanded to a thousand generations.}

\enubox{9 Which covenant he made with Abraham, and his oath unto Isaac;}

\enubox{10 And confirmed the same unto Jacob for a law, and to Israel for an everlasting covenant:}

\enubox{11 Saying, Unto thee will I give the land of Canaan, the lot of your inheritance:}

\enubox{12 When they were but a few men in number; yea, very few, and strangers in it.}

\enubox{13 When they went from one nation to another, from one kingdom to another people;}

\enubox{14 He suffered no man to do them wrong: yea, he reproved kings for their sakes;}

\enubox{15 Saying, Touch not mine anointed, and do my prophets no harm.}

\enubox{16 Moreover he called for a famine upon the land: he brake the whole staff of bread.}

\enubox{17 He sent a man before them, even Joseph, who was sold for a servant:}

\enubox{18 Whose feet they hurt with fetters: he was laid in iron:}

\enubox{19 Until the time that his word came: the word of the LORD tried him.}

\enubox{20 The king sent and loosed him; even the ruler of the people, and let him go free.}

\enubox{21 He made him lord of his house, and ruler of all his substance:}

\enubox{22 To bind his princes at his pleasure; and teach his senators wisdom.}

\enubox{23 Israel also came into Egypt; and Jacob sojourned in the land of Ham.}

\enubox{24 And he increased his people greatly; and made them stronger than their enemies.}

\enubox{25 He turned their heart to hate his people, to deal subtilly with his servants.}

\enubox{26 He sent Moses his servant; and Aaron whom he had chosen.}

\enubox{27 They shewed his signs among them, and wonders in the land of Ham.}

\enubox{28 He sent darkness, and made it dark; and they rebelled not against his word.}

\enubox{29 He turned their waters into blood, and slew their fish.}

\enubox{30 Their land brought forth frogs in abundance, in the chambers of their kings.}

\enubox{31 He spake, and there came divers sorts of flies, and lice in all their coasts.}

\enubox{32 He gave them hail for rain, and flaming fire in their land.}

\enubox{33 He smote their vines also and their fig trees; and brake the trees of their coasts.}

\enubox{34 He spake, and the locusts came, and caterpillers, and that without number,}

\enubox{35 And did eat up all the herbs in their land, and devoured the fruit of their ground.}

\enubox{36 He smote also all the firstborn in their land, the chief of all their strength.}

\enubox{37 He brought them forth also with silver and gold: and there was not one feeble person among their tribes.}

\enubox{38 Egypt was glad when they departed: for the fear of them fell upon them.}

\enubox{39 He spread a cloud for a covering; and fire to give light in the night.}

\enubox{40 The people asked, and he brought quails, and satisfied them with the bread of heaven.}

\enubox{41 He opened the rock, and the waters gushed out; they ran in the dry places like a river.}

\enubox{42 For he remembered his holy promise, and Abraham his servant.}

\enubox{43 And he brought forth his people with joy, and his chosen with gladness:}

\enubox{44 And gave them the lands of the heathen: and they inherited the labour of the people;}

\enubox{45 That they might observe his statutes, and keep his laws. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 106}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M509x515S18720491x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{2 Who can utter the mighty acts of the LORD? who can shew forth all his praise?}

\enubox{3 Blessed are they that keep judgment, and he that doeth righteousness at all times.}

\enubox{4 Remember me, O LORD, with the favour that thou bearest unto thy people: O visit me with thy salvation;}

\enubox{5 That I may see the good of thy chosen, that I may rejoice in the gladness of thy nation, that I may glory with thine inheritance.}

\enubox{6 We have sinned with our fathers, we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly.}

\enubox{7 Our fathers understood not thy wonders in Egypt; they remembered not the multitude of thy mercies; but provoked him at the sea, even at the Red sea.}

\enubox{8 Nevertheless he saved them for his name's sake, that he might make his mighty power to be known.}

\enubox{9 He rebuked the Red sea also, and it was dried up: so he led them through the depths, as through the wilderness.}

\enubox{10 And he saved them from the hand of him that hated them, and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.}

\enubox{11 And the waters covered their enemies: there was not one of them left.}

\enubox{12 Then believed they his words; they sang his praise.}

\enubox{13 They soon forgat his works; they waited not for his counsel:}

\enubox{14 But lusted exceedingly in the wilderness, and tempted God in the desert.}

\enubox{15 And he gave them their request; but sent leanness into their soul.}

\enubox{16 They envied Moses also in the camp, and Aaron the saint of the LORD.}

\enubox{17 The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan and covered the company of Abiram.}

\enubox{18 And a fire was kindled in their company; the flame burned up the wicked.}

\enubox{19 They made a calf in Horeb, and worshipped the molten image.}

\enubox{20 Thus they changed their glory into the similitude of an ox that eateth grass.}

\enubox{21 They forgat God their saviour, which had done great things in Egypt;}

\enubox{22 Wondrous works in the land of Ham, and terrible things by the Red sea.}

\enubox{23 Therefore he said that he would destroy them, had not Moses his chosen stood before him in the breach, to turn away his wrath, lest he should destroy them.}

\enubox{24 Yea, they despised the pleasant land, they believed not his word:}

\enubox{25 But murmured in their tents, and hearkened not unto the voice of the LORD.}

\enubox{26 Therefore he lifted up his hand against them, to overthrow them in the wilderness:}

\enubox{27 To overthrow their seed also among the nations, and to scatter them in the lands.}

\enubox{28 They joined themselves also unto Baalpeor, and ate the sacrifices of the dead.}

\enubox{29 Thus they provoked him to anger with their inventions: and the plague brake in upon them.}

\enubox{30 Then stood up Phinehas, and executed judgment: and so the plague was stayed.}

\enubox{31 And that was counted unto him for righteousness unto all generations for evermore.}

\enubox{32 They angered him also at the waters of strife, so that it went ill with Moses for their sakes:}

\enubox{33 Because they provoked his spirit, so that he spake unadvisedly with his lips.}

\enubox{34 They did not destroy the nations, concerning whom the LORD commanded them:}

\enubox{35 But were mingled among the heathen, and learned their works.}

\enubox{36 And they served their idols: which were a snare unto them.}

\enubox{37 Yea, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters unto devils,}

\enubox{38 And shed innocent blood, even the blood of their sons and of their daughters, whom they sacrificed unto the idols of Canaan: and the land was polluted with blood.}

\enubox{39 Thus were they defiled with their own works, and went a whoring with their own inventions.}

\enubox{40 Therefore was the wrath of the LORD kindled against his people, insomuch that he abhorred his own inheritance.}

\enubox{41 And he gave them into the hand of the heathen; and they that hated them ruled over them.}

\enubox{42 Their enemies also oppressed them, and they were brought into subjection under their hand.}

\enubox{43 Many times did he deliver them; but they provoked him with their counsel, and were brought low for their iniquity.}

\enubox{44 Nevertheless he regarded their affliction, when he heard their cry:}

\enubox{45 And he remembered for them his covenant, and repented according to the multitude of his mercies.}

\enubox{46 He made them also to be pitied of all those that carried them captives.}

\enubox{47 Save us, O LORD our God, and gather us from among the heathen, to give thanks unto thy holy name, and to triumph in thy praise.}

\enubox{48 Blessed be the LORD God of Israel from everlasting to everlasting: and let all the people say, Amen. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 107}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x514S1a520490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O give thanks unto the LORD, for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{2 Let the redeemed of the LORD say so, whom he hath redeemed from the hand of the enemy;}

\enubox{3 And gathered them out of the lands, from the east, and from the west, from the north, and from the south.}

\enubox{4 They wandered in the wilderness in a solitary way; they found no city to dwell in.}

\enubox{5 Hungry and thirsty, their soul fainted in them.}

\enubox{6 Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he delivered them out of their distresses.}

\enubox{7 And he led them forth by the right way, that they might go to a city of habitation.}

\enubox{8 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men!}

\enubox{9 For he satisfieth the longing soul, and filleth the hungry soul with goodness.}

\enubox{10 Such as sit in darkness and in the shadow of death, being bound in affliction and iron;}

\enubox{11 Because they rebelled against the words of God, and contemned the counsel of the most High:}

\enubox{12 Therefore he brought down their heart with labour; they fell down, and there was none to help.}

\enubox{13 Then they cried unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saved them out of their distresses.}

\enubox{14 He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death, and brake their bands in sunder.}

\enubox{15 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men!}

\enubox{16 For he hath broken the gates of brass, and cut the bars of iron in sunder.}

\enubox{17 Fools because of their transgression, and because of their iniquities, are afflicted.}

\enubox{18 Their soul abhorreth all manner of meat; and they draw near unto the gates of death.}

\enubox{19 Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he saveth them out of their distresses.}

\enubox{20 He sent his word, and healed them, and delivered them from their destructions.}

\enubox{21 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men!}

\enubox{22 And let them sacrifice the sacrifices of thanksgiving, and declare his works with rejoicing.}

\enubox{23 They that go down to the sea in ships, that do business in great waters;}

\enubox{24 These see the works of the LORD, and his wonders in the deep.}

\enubox{25 For he commandeth, and raiseth the stormy wind, which lifteth up the waves thereof.}

\enubox{26 They mount up to the heaven, they go down again to the depths: their soul is melted because of trouble.}

\enubox{27 They reel to and fro, and stagger like a drunken man, and are at their wit's end.}

\enubox{28 Then they cry unto the LORD in their trouble, and he bringeth them out of their distresses.}

\enubox{29 He maketh the storm a calm, so that the waves thereof are still.}

\enubox{30 Then are they glad because they be quiet; so he bringeth them unto their desired haven.}

\enubox{31 Oh that men would praise the LORD for his goodness, and for his wonderful works to the children of men!}

\enubox{32 Let them exalt him also in the congregation of the people, and praise him in the assembly of the elders.}

\enubox{33 He turneth rivers into a wilderness, and the watersprings into dry ground;}

\enubox{34 A fruitful land into barrenness, for the wickedness of them that dwell therein.}

\enubox{35 He turneth the wilderness into a standing water, and dry ground into watersprings.}

\enubox{36 And there he maketh the hungry to dwell, that they may prepare a city for habitation;}

\enubox{37 And sow the fields, and plant vineyards, which may yield fruits of increase.}

\enubox{38 He blesseth them also, so that they are multiplied greatly; and suffereth not their cattle to decrease.}

\enubox{39 Again, they are minished and brought low through oppression, affliction, and sorrow.}

\enubox{40 He poureth contempt upon princes, and causeth them to wander in the wilderness, where there is no way.}

\enubox{41 Yet setteth he the poor on high from affliction, and maketh him families like a flock.}

\enubox{42 The righteous shall see it, and rejoice: and all iniquity shall stop her mouth.}

\enubox{43 Whoso is wise, and will observe these things, even they shall understand the lovingkindness of the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 108}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x514S1bb20490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O god, my heart is fixed; I will sing and give praise, even with my glory.}

\enubox{2 Awake, psaltery and harp: I myself will awake early.}

\enubox{3 I will praise thee, O LORD, among the people: and I will sing praises unto thee among the nations.}

\enubox{4 For thy mercy is great above the heavens: and thy truth reacheth unto the clouds.}

\enubox{5 Be thou exalted, O God, above the heavens: and thy glory above all the earth;}

\enubox{6 That thy beloved may be delivered: save with thy right hand, and answer me.}

\enubox{7 God hath spoken in his holiness; I will rejoice, I will divide Shechem, and mete out the valley of Succoth.}

\enubox{8 Gilead is mine; Manasseh is mine; Ephraim also is the strength of mine head; Judah is my lawgiver;}

\enubox{9 Moab is my washpot; over Edom will I cast out my shoe; over Philistia will I triumph.}

\enubox{10 Who will bring me into the strong city? who will lead me into Edom?}

\enubox{11 Wilt not thou, O God, who hast cast us off? and wilt not thou, O God, go forth with our hosts?}

\enubox{12 Give us help from trouble: for vain is the help of man.}

\enubox{13 Through God we shall do valiantly: for he it is that shall tread down our enemies.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 109}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x515S1ce20489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Hold not thy peace, O God of my praise;}

\enubox{2 For the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of the deceitful are opened against me: they have spoken against me with a lying tongue.}

\enubox{3 They compassed me about also with words of hatred; and fought against me without a cause.}

\enubox{4 For my love they are my adversaries: but I give myself unto prayer.}

\enubox{5 And they have rewarded me evil for good, and hatred for my love.}

\enubox{6 Set thou a wicked man over him: and let Satan stand at his right hand.}

\enubox{7 When he shall be judged, let him be condemned: and let his prayer become sin.}

\enubox{8 Let his days be few; and let another take his office.}

\enubox{9 Let his children be fatherless, and his wife a widow.}

\enubox{10 Let his children be continually vagabonds, and beg: let them seek their bread also out of their desolate places.}

\enubox{11 Let the extortioner catch all that he hath; and let the strangers spoil his labour.}

\enubox{12 Let there be none to extend mercy unto him: neither let there be any to favour his fatherless children.}

\enubox{13 Let his posterity be cut off; and in the generation following let their name be blotted out.}

\enubox{14 Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered with the LORD; and let not the sin of his mother be blotted out.}

\enubox{15 Let them be before the LORD continually, that he may cut off the memory of them from the earth.}

\enubox{16 Because that he remembered not to shew mercy, but persecuted the poor and needy man, that he might even slay the broken in heart.}

\enubox{17 As he loved cursing, so let it come unto him: as he delighted not in blessing, so let it be far from him.}

\enubox{18 As he clothed himself with cursing like as with his garment, so let it come into his bowels like water, and like oil into his bones.}

\enubox{19 Let it be unto him as the garment which covereth him, and for a girdle wherewith he is girded continually.}

\enubox{20 Let this be the reward of mine adversaries from the LORD, and of them that speak evil against my soul.}

\enubox{21 But do thou for me, O GOD the Lord, for thy name's sake: because thy mercy is good, deliver thou me.}

\enubox{22 For I am poor and needy, and my heart is wounded within me.}

\enubox{23 I am gone like the shadow when it declineth: I am tossed up and down as the locust.}

\enubox{24 My knees are weak through fasting; and my flesh faileth of fatness.}

\enubox{25 I became also a reproach unto them: when they looked upon me they shaked their heads.}

\enubox{26 Help me, O LORD my God: O save me according to thy mercy:}

\enubox{27 That they may know that this is thy hand; that thou, LORD, hast done it.}

\enubox{28 Let them curse, but bless thou: when they arise, let them be ashamed; but let thy servant rejoice.}

\enubox{29 Let mine adversaries be clothed with shame, and let them cover themselves with their own confusion, as with a mantle.}

\enubox{30 I will greatly praise the LORD with my mouth; yea, I will praise him among the multitude.}

\enubox{31 For he shall stand at the right hand of the poor, to save him from those that condemn his soul.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 110}

\enubox{1 The LORD said unto my Lord, Sit thou at my right hand, until I make thine enemies thy footstool.}

\enubox{2 The LORD shall send the rod of thy strength out of Zion: rule thou in the midst of thine enemies.}

\enubox{3 Thy people shall be willing in the day of thy power, in the beauties of holiness from the womb of the morning: thou hast the dew of thy youth.}

\enubox{4 The LORD hath sworn, and will not repent, Thou art a priest for ever after the order of Melchizedek.}

\enubox{5 The Lord at thy right hand shall strike through kings in the day of his wrath.}

\enubox{6 He shall judge among the heathen, he shall fill the places with the dead bodies; he shall wound the heads over many countries.}

\enubox{7 He shall drink of the brook in the way: therefore shall he lift up the head.}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. I will praise the LORD with my whole heart, in the assembly of the upright, and in the congregation.}

\enubox{2 The works of the LORD are great, sought out of all them that have pleasure therein.}

\enubox{3 His work is honourable and glorious: and his righteousness endureth for ever.}

\enubox{4 He hath made his wonderful works to be remembered: the LORD is gracious and full of compassion.}

\enubox{5 He hath given meat unto them that fear him: he will ever be mindful of his covenant.}

\enubox{6 He hath shewed his people the power of his works, that he may give them the heritage of the heathen.}

\enubox{7 The works of his hands are verity and judgment; all his commandments are sure.}

\enubox{8 They stand fast for ever and ever, and are done in truth and uprightness.}

\enubox{9 He sent redemption unto his people: he hath commanded his covenant for ever: holy and reverend is his name.}

\enubox{10 The fear of the LORD is the beginning of wisdom: a good understanding have all they that do his commandments: his praise endureth for ever.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 112}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Blessed is the man that feareth the LORD, that delighteth greatly in his commandments.}

\enubox{2 His seed shall be mighty upon earth: the generation of the upright shall be blessed.}

\enubox{3 Wealth and riches shall be in his house: and his righteousness endureth for ever.}

\enubox{4 Unto the upright there ariseth light in the darkness: he is gracious, and full of compassion, and righteous.}

\enubox{5 A good man sheweth favour, and lendeth: he will guide his affairs with discretion.}

\enubox{6 Surely he shall not be moved for ever: the righteous shall be in everlasting remembrance.}

\enubox{7 He shall not be afraid of evil tidings: his heart is fixed, trusting in the LORD.}

\enubox{8 His heart is established, he shall not be afraid, until he see his desire upon his enemies.}

\enubox{9 He hath dispersed, he hath given to the poor; his righteousness endureth for ever; his horn shall be exalted with honour.}

\enubox{10 The wicked shall see it, and be grieved; he shall gnash with his teeth, and melt away: the desire of the wicked shall perish.}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Praise, O ye servants of the LORD, praise the name of the LORD.}

\enubox{2 Blessed be the name of the LORD from this time forth and for evermore.}

\enubox{3 From the rising of the sun unto the going down of the same the LORD's name is to be praised.}

\enubox{4 The LORD is high above all nations, and his glory above the heavens.}

\enubox{5 Who is like unto the LORD our God, who dwelleth on high,}

\enubox{6 Who humbleth himself to behold the things that are in heaven, and in the earth!}

\enubox{7 He raiseth up the poor out of the dust, and lifteth the needy out of the dunghill;}

\enubox{8 That he may set him with princes, even with the princes of his people.}

\enubox{9 He maketh the barren woman to keep house, and to be a joyful mother of children. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 114}

\enubox{1 When Israel went out of Egypt, the house of Jacob from a people of strange language;}

\enubox{2 Judah was his sanctuary, and Israel his dominion.}

\enubox{3 The sea saw it, and fled: Jordan was driven back.}

\enubox{4 The mountains skipped like rams, and the little hills like lambs.}

\enubox{5 What ailed thee, O thou sea, that thou fleddest? thou Jordan, that thou wast driven back?}

\enubox{6 Ye mountains, that ye skipped like rams; and ye little hills, like lambs?}

\enubox{7 Tremble, thou earth, at the presence of the Lord, at the presence of the God of Jacob;}

\enubox{8 Which turned the rock into a standing water, the flint into a fountain of waters.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 115}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M513x518S22114487x483S15d00494x491

\enubox{1 Not unto us, O LORD, not unto us, but unto thy name give glory, for thy mercy, and for thy truth's sake.}

\enubox{2 Wherefore should the heathen say, Where is now their God?}

\enubox{3 But our God is in the heavens: he hath done whatsoever he hath pleased.}

\enubox{4 Their idols are silver and gold, the work of men's hands.}

\enubox{5 They have mouths, but they speak not: eyes have they, but they see not:}

\enubox{6 They have ears, but they hear not: noses have they, but they smell not:}

\enubox{7 They have hands, but they handle not: feet have they, but they walk not: neither speak they through their throat.}

\enubox{8 They that make them are like unto them; so is every one that trusteth in them.}

\enubox{9 O Israel, trust thou in the LORD: he is their help and their shield.}

\enubox{10 O house of Aaron, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield.}

\enubox{11 Ye that fear the LORD, trust in the LORD: he is their help and their shield.}

\enubox{12 The LORD hath been mindful of us: he will bless us; he will bless the house of Israel; he will bless the house of Aaron.}

\enubox{13 He will bless them that fear the LORD, both small and great.}

\enubox{14 The LORD shall increase you more and more, you and your children.}

\enubox{15 Ye are blessed of the LORD which made heaven and earth.}

\enubox{16 The heaven, even the heavens, are the LORD's: but the earth hath he given to the children of men.}

\enubox{17 The dead praise not the LORD, neither any that go down into silence.}

\enubox{18 But we will bless the LORD from this time forth and for evermore. Praise the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 116}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M520x522S18700502x492S2e00e480x479

\enubox{1 I love the LORD, because he hath heard my voice and my supplications.}

\enubox{2 Because he hath inclined his ear unto me, therefore will I call upon him as long as I live.}

\enubox{3 The sorrows of death compassed me, and the pains of hell gat hold upon me: I found trouble and sorrow.}

\enubox{4 Then called I upon the name of the LORD; O LORD, I beseech thee, deliver my soul.}

\enubox{5 Gracious is the LORD, and righteous; yea, our God is merciful.}

\enubox{6 The LORD preserveth the simple: I was brought low, and he helped me.}

\enubox{7 Return unto thy rest, O my soul; for the LORD hath dealt bountifully with thee.}

\enubox{8 For thou hast delivered my soul from death, mine eyes from tears, and my feet from falling.}

\enubox{9 I will walk before the LORD in the land of the living.}

\enubox{10 I believed, therefore have I spoken: I was greatly afflicted:}

\enubox{11 I said in my haste, All men are liars.}

\enubox{12 What shall I render unto the LORD for all his benefits toward me?}

\enubox{13 I will take the cup of salvation, and call upon the name of the LORD.}

\enubox{14 I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people.}

\enubox{15 Precious in the sight of the LORD is the death of his saints.}

\enubox{16 O LORD, truly I am thy servant; I am thy servant, and the son of thine handmaid: thou hast loosed my bonds.}

\enubox{17 I will offer to thee the sacrifice of thanksgiving, and will call upon the name of the LORD.}

\enubox{18 I will pay my vows unto the LORD now in the presence of all his people.}

\enubox{19 In the courts of the LORD's house, in the midst of thee, O Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 118}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M523x522S1bb00502x492S2e00e478x479 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: because his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{2 Let Israel now say, that his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{3 Let the house of Aaron now say, that his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{4 Let them now that fear the LORD say, that his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{5 I called upon the LORD in distress: the LORD answered me, and set me in a large place.}

\enubox{6 The LORD is on my side; I will not fear: what can man do unto me?}

\enubox{7 The LORD taketh my part with them that help me: therefore shall I see my desire upon them that hate me.}

\enubox{8 It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in man.}

\enubox{9 It is better to trust in the LORD than to put confidence in princes.}

\enubox{10 All nations compassed me about: but in the name of the LORD will I destroy them.}

\enubox{11 They compassed me about; yea, they compassed me about: but in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.}

\enubox{12 They compassed me about like bees: they are quenched as the fire of thorns: for in the name of the LORD I will destroy them.}

\enubox{13 Thou hast thrust sore at me that I might fall: but the LORD helped me.}

\enubox{14 The LORD is my strength and song, and is become my salvation.}

\enubox{15 The voice of rejoicing and salvation is in the tabernacles of the righteous: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly.}

\enubox{16 The right hand of the LORD is exalted: the right hand of the LORD doeth valiantly.}

\enubox{17 I shall not die, but live, and declare the works of the LORD.}

\enubox{18 The LORD hath chastened me sore: but he hath not given me over unto death.}

\enubox{19 Open to me the gates of righteousness: I will go into them, and I will praise the LORD:}

\enubox{20 This gate of the LORD, into which the righteous shall enter.}

\enubox{21 I will praise thee: for thou hast heard me, and art become my salvation.}

\enubox{22 The stone which the builders refused is become the head stone of the corner.}

\enubox{23 This is the LORD's doing; it is marvellous in our eyes.}

\enubox{24 This is the day which the LORD hath made; we will rejoice and be glad in it.}

\enubox{25 Save now, I beseech thee, O LORD: O LORD, I beseech thee, send now prosperity.}

\enubox{26 Blessed be he that cometh in the name of the LORD: we have blessed you out of the house of the LORD.}

\enubox{27 God is the LORD, which hath shewed us light: bind the sacrifice with cords, even unto the horns of the altar.}

\enubox{28 Thou art my God, and I will praise thee: thou art my God, I will exalt thee.}

\enubox{29 O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 119}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M524x522S1ce00502x490S2e00e477x479 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Blessed are the undefiled in the way, who walk in the law of the LORD.}

\enubox{2 Blessed are they that keep his testimonies, and that seek him with the whole heart.}

\enubox{3 They also do no iniquity: they walk in his ways.}

\enubox{4 Thou hast commanded us to keep thy precepts diligently.}

\enubox{5 O that my ways were directed to keep thy statutes!}

\enubox{6 Then shall I not be ashamed, when I have respect unto all thy commandments.}

\enubox{7 I will praise thee with uprightness of heart, when I shall have learned thy righteous judgments.}

\enubox{8 I will keep thy statutes: O forsake me not utterly.}

\enubox{9 Wherewithal shall a young man cleanse his way? by taking heed thereto according to thy word.}

\enubox{10 With my whole heart have I sought thee: O let me not wander from thy commandments.}

\enubox{11 Thy word have I hid in mine heart, that I might not sin against thee.}

\enubox{12 Blessed art thou, O LORD: teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{13 With my lips have I declared all the judgments of thy mouth.}

\enubox{14 I have rejoiced in the way of thy testimonies, as much as in all riches.}

\enubox{15 I will meditate in thy precepts, and have respect unto thy ways.}

\enubox{16 I will delight myself in thy statutes: I will not forget thy word.}

\enubox{17 Deal bountifully with thy servant, that I may live, and keep thy word.}

\enubox{18 Open thou mine eyes, that I may behold wondrous things out of thy law.}

\enubox{19 I am a stranger in the earth: hide not thy commandments from me.}

\enubox{20 My soul breaketh for the longing that it hath unto thy judgments at all times.}

\enubox{21 Thou hast rebuked the proud that are cursed, which do err from thy commandments.}

\enubox{22 Remove from me reproach and contempt; for I have kept thy testimonies.}

\enubox{23 Princes also did sit and speak against me: but thy servant did meditate in thy statutes.}

\enubox{24 Thy testimonies also are my delight and my counsellors.}

\enubox{25 My soul cleaveth unto the dust: quicken thou me according to thy word.}

\enubox{26 I have declared my ways, and thou heardest me: teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{27 Make me to understand the way of thy precepts: so shall I talk of thy wondrous works.}

\enubox{28 My soul melteth for heaviness: strengthen thou me according unto thy word.}

\enubox{29 Remove from me the way of lying: and grant me thy law graciously.}

\enubox{30 I have chosen the way of truth: thy judgments have I laid before me.}

\enubox{31 I have stuck unto thy testimonies: O LORD, put me not to shame.}

\enubox{32 I will run the way of thy commandments, when thou shalt enlarge my heart.}

\enubox{33 Teach me, O LORD, the way of thy statutes; and I shall keep it unto the end.}

\enubox{34 Give me understanding, and I shall keep thy law; yea, I shall observe it with my whole heart.}

\enubox{35 Make me to go in the path of thy commandments; for therein do I delight.}

\enubox{36 Incline my heart unto thy testimonies, and not to covetousness.}

\enubox{37 Turn away mine eyes from beholding vanity; and quicken thou me in thy way.}

\enubox{38 Stablish thy word unto thy servant, who is devoted to thy fear.}

\enubox{39 Turn away my reproach which I fear: for thy judgments are good.}

\enubox{40 Behold, I have longed after thy precepts: quicken me in thy righteousness.}

\enubox{41 Let thy mercies come also unto me, O LORD, even thy salvation, according to thy word.}

\enubox{42 So shall I have wherewith to answer him that reproacheth me: for I trust in thy word.}

\enubox{43 And take not the word of truth utterly out of my mouth; for I have hoped in thy judgments.}

\enubox{44 So shall I keep thy law continually for ever and ever.}

\enubox{45 And I will walk at liberty: for I seek thy precepts.}

\enubox{46 I will speak of thy testimonies also before kings, and will not be ashamed.}

\enubox{47 And I will delight myself in thy commandments, which I have loved.}

\enubox{48 My hands also will I lift up unto thy commandments, which I have loved; and I will meditate in thy statutes.}

\enubox{49 Remember the word unto thy servant, upon which thou hast caused me to hope.}

\enubox{50 This is my comfort in my affliction: for thy word hath quickened me.}

\enubox{51 The proud have had me greatly in derision: yet have I not declined from thy law.}

\enubox{52 I remembered thy judgments of old, O LORD; and have comforted myself.}

\enubox{53 Horror hath taken hold upon me because of the wicked that forsake thy law.}

\enubox{54 Thy statutes have been my songs in the house of my pilgrimage.}

\enubox{55 I have remembered thy name, O LORD, in the night, and have kept thy law.}

\enubox{56 This I had, because I kept thy precepts.}

\enubox{57 Thou art my portion, O LORD: I have said that I would keep thy words.}

\enubox{58 I intreated thy favour with my whole heart: be merciful unto me according to thy word.}

\enubox{59 I thought on my ways, and turned my feet unto thy testimonies.}

\enubox{60 I made haste, and delayed not to keep thy commandments.}

\enubox{61 The bands of the wicked have robbed me: but I have not forgotten thy law.}

\enubox{62 At midnight I will rise to give thanks unto thee because of thy righteous judgments.}

\enubox{63 I am a companion of all them that fear thee, and of them that keep thy precepts.}

\enubox{64 The earth, O LORD, is full of thy mercy: teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{65 Thou hast dealt well with thy servant, O LORD, according unto thy word.}

\enubox{66 Teach me good judgment and knowledge: for I have believed thy commandments.}

\enubox{67 Before I was afflicted I went astray: but now have I kept thy word.}

\enubox{68 Thou art good, and doest good; teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{69 The proud have forged a lie against me: but I will keep thy precepts with my whole heart.}

\enubox{70 Their heart is as fat as grease; but I delight in thy law.}

\enubox{71 It is good for me that I have been afflicted; that I might learn thy statutes.}

\enubox{72 The law of thy mouth is better unto me than thousands of gold and silver.}

\enubox{73 Thy hands have made me and fashioned me: give me understanding, that I may learn thy commandments.}

\enubox{74 They that fear thee will be glad when they see me; because I have hoped in thy word.}

\enubox{75 I know, O LORD, that thy judgments are right, and that thou in faithfulness hast afflicted me.}

\enubox{76 Let, I pray thee, thy merciful kindness be for my comfort, according to thy word unto thy servant.}

\enubox{77 Let thy tender mercies come unto me, that I may live: for thy law is my delight.}

\enubox{78 Let the proud be ashamed; for they dealt perversely with me without a cause: but I will meditate in thy precepts.}

\enubox{79 Let those that fear thee turn unto me, and those that have known thy testimonies.}

\enubox{80 Let my heart be sound in thy statutes; that I be not ashamed.}

\enubox{81 My soul fainteth for thy salvation: but I hope in thy word.}

\enubox{82 Mine eyes fail for thy word, saying, When wilt thou comfort me?}

\enubox{83 For I am become like a bottle in the smoke; yet do I not forget thy statutes.}

\enubox{84 How many are the days of thy servant? when wilt thou execute judgment on them that persecute me?}

\enubox{85 The proud have digged pits for me, which are not after thy law.}

\enubox{86 All thy commandments are faithful: they persecute me wrongfully; help thou me.}

\enubox{87 They had almost consumed me upon earth; but I forsook not thy precepts.}

\enubox{88 Quicken me after thy lovingkindness; so shall I keep the testimony of thy mouth.}

\enubox{89 For ever, O LORD, thy word is settled in heaven.}

\enubox{90 Thy faithfulness is unto all generations: thou hast established the earth, and it abideth.}

\enubox{91 They continue this day according to thine ordinances: for all are thy servants.}

\enubox{92 Unless thy law had been my delights, I should then have perished in mine affliction.}

\enubox{93 I will never forget thy precepts: for with them thou hast quickened me.}

\enubox{94 I am thine, save me: for I have sought thy precepts.}

\enubox{95 The wicked have waited for me to destroy me: but I will consider thy testimonies.}

\enubox{96 I have seen an end of all perfection: but thy commandment is exceeding broad.}

\enubox{97 O how I love thy law! it is my meditation all the day.}

\enubox{98 Thou through thy commandments hast made me wiser than mine enemies: for they are ever with me.}

\enubox{99 I have more understanding than all my teachers: for thy testimonies are my meditation.}

\enubox{100 I understand more than the ancients, because I keep thy precepts.}

\enubox{101 I have refrained my feet from every evil way, that I might keep thy word.}

\enubox{102 I have not departed from thy judgments: for thou hast taught me.}

\enubox{103 How sweet are thy words unto my taste! yea, sweeter than honey to my mouth!}

\enubox{104 Through thy precepts I get understanding: therefore I hate every false way.}

\enubox{105 Thy word is a lamp unto my feet, and a light unto my path.}

\enubox{106 I have sworn, and I will perform it, that I will keep thy righteous judgments.}

\enubox{107 I am afflicted very much: quicken me, O LORD, according unto thy word.}

\enubox{108 Accept, I beseech thee, the freewill offerings of my mouth, O LORD, and teach me thy judgments.}

\enubox{109 My soul is continually in my hand: yet do I not forget thy law.}

\enubox{110 The wicked have laid a snare for me: yet I erred not from thy precepts.}

\enubox{111 Thy testimonies have I taken as an heritage for ever: for they are the rejoicing of my heart.}

\enubox{112 I have inclined mine heart to perform thy statutes alway, even unto the end.}

\enubox{113 I hate vain thoughts: but thy law do I love.}

\enubox{114 Thou art my hiding place and my shield: I hope in thy word.}

\enubox{115 Depart from me, ye evildoers: for I will keep the commandments of my God.}

\enubox{116 Uphold me according unto thy word, that I may live: and let me not be ashamed of my hope.}

\enubox{117 Hold thou me up, and I shall be safe: and I will have respect unto thy statutes continually.}

\enubox{118 Thou hast trodden down all them that err from thy statutes: for their deceit is falsehood.}

\enubox{119 Thou puttest away all the wicked of the earth like dross: therefore I love thy testimonies.}

\enubox{120 My flesh trembleth for fear of thee; and I am afraid of thy judgments.}

\enubox{121 I have done judgment and justice: leave me not to mine oppressors.}

\enubox{122 Be surety for thy servant for good: let not the proud oppress me.}

\enubox{123 Mine eyes fail for thy salvation, and for the word of thy righteousness.}

\enubox{124 Deal with thy servant according unto thy mercy, and teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{125 I am thy servant; give me understanding, that I may know thy testimonies.}

\enubox{126 It is time for thee, LORD, to work: for they have made void thy law.}

\enubox{127 Therefore I love thy commandments above gold; yea, above fine gold.}

\enubox{128 Therefore I esteem all thy precepts concerning all things to be right; and I hate every false way.}

\enubox{129 Thy testimonies are wonderful: therefore doth my soul keep them.}

\enubox{130 The entrance of thy words giveth light; it giveth understanding unto the simple.}

\enubox{131 I opened my mouth, and panted: for I longed for thy commandments.}

\enubox{132 Look thou upon me, and be merciful unto me, as thou usest to do unto those that love thy name.}

\enubox{133 Order my steps in thy word: and let not any iniquity have dominion over me.}

\enubox{134 Deliver me from the oppression of man: so will I keep thy precepts.}

\enubox{135 Make thy face to shine upon thy servant; and teach me thy statutes.}

\enubox{136 Rivers of waters run down mine eyes, because they keep not thy law.}

\enubox{137 Righteous art thou, O LORD, and upright are thy judgments.}

\enubox{138 Thy testimonies that thou hast commanded are righteous and very faithful.}

\enubox{139 My zeal hath consumed me, because mine enemies have forgotten thy words.}

\enubox{140 Thy word is very pure: therefore thy servant loveth it.}

\enubox{141 I am small and despised: yet do not I forget thy precepts.}

\enubox{142 Thy righteousness is an everlasting righteousness, and thy law is the truth.}

\enubox{143 Trouble and anguish have taken hold on me: yet thy commandments are my delights.}

\enubox{144 The righteousness of thy testimonies is everlasting: give me understanding, and I shall live.}

\enubox{145 I cried with my whole heart; hear me, O LORD: I will keep thy statutes.}

\enubox{146 I cried unto thee; save me, and I shall keep thy testimonies.}

\enubox{147 I prevented the dawning of the morning, and cried: I hoped in thy word.}

\enubox{148 Mine eyes prevent the night watches, that I might meditate in thy word.}

\enubox{149 Hear my voice according unto thy lovingkindness: O LORD, quicken me according to thy judgment.}

\enubox{150 They draw nigh that follow after mischief: they are far from thy law.}

\enubox{151 Thou art near, O LORD; and all thy commandments are truth.}

\enubox{152 Concerning thy testimonies, I have known of old that thou hast founded them for ever.}

\enubox{153 Consider mine affliction, and deliver me: for I do not forget thy law.}

\enubox{154 Plead my cause, and deliver me: quicken me according to thy word.}

\enubox{155 Salvation is far from the wicked: for they seek not thy statutes.}

\enubox{156 Great are thy tender mercies, O LORD: quicken me according to thy judgments.}

\enubox{157 Many are my persecutors and mine enemies; yet do I not decline from thy testimonies.}

\enubox{158 I beheld the transgressors, and was grieved; because they kept not thy word.}

\enubox{159 Consider how I love thy precepts: quicken me, O LORD, according to thy lovingkindness.}

\enubox{160 Thy word is true from the beginning: and every one of thy righteous judgments endureth for ever.}

\enubox{161 Princes have persecuted me without a cause: but my heart standeth in awe of thy word.}

\enubox{162 I rejoice at thy word, as one that findeth great spoil.}

\enubox{163 I hate and abhor lying: but thy law do I love.}

\enubox{164 Seven times a day do I praise thee because of thy righteous judgments.}

\enubox{165 Great peace have they which love thy law: and nothing shall offend them.}

\enubox{166 LORD, I have hoped for thy salvation, and done thy commandments.}

\enubox{167 My soul hath kept thy testimonies; and I love them exceedingly.}

\enubox{168 I have kept thy precepts and thy testimonies: for all my ways are before thee.}

\enubox{169 Let my cry come near before thee, O LORD: give me understanding according to thy word.}

\enubox{170 Let my supplication come before thee: deliver me according to thy word.}

\enubox{171 My lips shall utter praise, when thou hast taught me thy statutes.}

\enubox{172 My tongue shall speak of thy word: for all thy commandments are righteousness.}

\enubox{173 Let thine hand help me; for I have chosen thy precepts.}

\enubox{174 I have longed for thy salvation, O LORD; and thy law is my delight.}

\enubox{175 Let my soul live, and it shall praise thee; and let thy judgments help me.}

\enubox{176 I have gone astray like a lost sheep; seek thy servant; for I do not forget thy commandments.}

\enubox{\bf Chapter 120}

\enubox{1 In my distress I cried unto the LORD, and he heard me.}

\enubox{2 Deliver my soul, O LORD, from lying lips, and from a deceitful tongue.}

\enubox{3 What shall be given unto thee? or what shall be done unto thee, thou false tongue?}

\enubox{4 Sharp arrows of the mighty, with coals of juniper.}

\enubox{5 Woe is me, that I sojourn in Mesech, that I dwell in the tents of Kedar!}

\enubox{6 My soul hath long dwelt with him that hateth peace.}

\enubox{7 I am for peace: but when I speak, they are for war.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 121}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M517x515S1e020494x485S21802484x497 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills, from whence cometh my help.}

\enubox{2 My help cometh from the LORD, which made heaven and earth.}

\enubox{3 He will not suffer thy foot to be moved: he that keepeth thee will not slumber.}

\enubox{4 Behold, he that keepeth Israel shall neither slumber nor sleep.}

\enubox{5 The LORD is thy keeper: the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.}

\enubox{6 The sun shall not smite thee by day, nor the moon by night.}

\enubox{7 The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil: he shall preserve thy soul.}

\enubox{8 The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in from this time forth, and even for evermore.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 122}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M518x528S10e50485x472S22f04483x514S26606488x501 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I was glad when they said unto me, Let us go into the house of the LORD.}

\enubox{2 Our feet shall stand within thy gates, O Jerusalem.}

\enubox{3 Jerusalem is builded as a city that is compact together:}

\enubox{4 Whither the tribes go up, the tribes of the LORD, unto the testimony of Israel, to give thanks unto the name of the LORD.}

\enubox{5 For there are set thrones of judgment, the thrones of the house of David.}

\enubox{6 Pray for the peace of Jerusalem: they shall prosper that love thee.}

\enubox{7 Peace be within thy walls, and prosperity within thy palaces.}

\enubox{8 For my brethren and companions' sakes, I will now say, Peace be within thee.}

\enubox{9 Because of the house of the LORD our God I will seek thy good.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 123}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M519x517S12420481x487S22114493x484 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Unto thee lift I up mine eyes, O thou that dwellest in the heavens.}

\enubox{2 Behold, as the eyes of servants look unto the hand of their masters, and as the eyes of a maiden unto the hand of her mistress; so our eyes wait upon the LORD our God, until that he have mercy upon us.}

\enubox{3 Have mercy upon us, O LORD, have mercy upon us: for we are exceedingly filled with contempt.}

\enubox{4 Our soul is exceedingly filled with the scorning of those that are at ease, and with the contempt of the proud.}

\enubox{1 They that trust in the LORD shall be as mount Zion, which cannot be removed, but abideth for ever.}

\enubox{2 As the mountains are round about Jerusalem, so the LORD is round about his people from henceforth even for ever.}

\enubox{3 For the rod of the wicked shall not rest upon the lot of the righteous; lest the righteous put forth their hands unto iniquity.}

\enubox{4 Do good, O LORD, unto those that be good, and to them that are upright in their hearts.}

\enubox{5 As for such as turn aside unto their crooked ways, the LORD shall lead them forth with the workers of iniquity: but peace shall be upon Israel.}

\enubox{1 When the LORD turned again the captivity of Zion, we were like them that dream.}

\enubox{2 Then was our mouth filled with laughter, and our tongue with singing: then said they among the heathen, The LORD hath done great things for them.}

\enubox{3 The LORD hath done great things for us; whereof we are glad.}

\enubox{4 Turn again our captivity, O LORD, as the streams in the south.}

\enubox{5 They that sow in tears shall reap in joy.}

\enubox{6 He that goeth forth and weepeth, bearing precious seed, shall doubtless come again with rejoicing, bringing his sheaves with him.}

\enubox{1 Lord, my heart is not haughty, nor mine eyes lofty: neither do I exercise myself in great matters, or in things too high for me.}

\enubox{2 Surely I have behaved and quieted myself, as a child that is weaned of his mother: my soul is even as a weaned child.}

\enubox{3 Let Israel hope in the LORD from henceforth and for ever.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 132}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M508x515S10e00493x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Lord, remember David, and all his afflictions:}

\enubox{2 How he sware unto the LORD, and vowed unto the mighty God of Jacob;}

\enubox{3 Surely I will not come into the tabernacle of my house, nor go up into my bed;}

\enubox{4 I will not give sleep to mine eyes, or slumber to mine eyelids,}

\enubox{5 Until I find out a place for the LORD, an habitation for the mighty God of Jacob.}

\enubox{6 Lo, we heard of it at Ephratah: we found it in the fields of the wood.}

\enubox{7 We will go into his tabernacles: we will worship at his footstool.}

\enubox{8 Arise, O LORD, into thy rest; thou, and the ark of thy strength.}

\enubox{9 Let thy priests be clothed with righteousness; and let thy saints shout for joy.}

\enubox{10 For thy servant David's sake turn not away the face of thine anointed.}

\enubox{11 The LORD hath sworn in truth unto David; he will not turn from it; Of the fruit of thy body will I set upon thy throne.}

\enubox{12 If thy children will keep my covenant and my testimony that I shall teach them, their children shall also sit upon thy throne for evermore.}

\enubox{13 For the LORD hath chosen Zion; he hath desired it for his habitation.}

\enubox{14 This is my rest for ever: here will I dwell; for I have desired it.}

\enubox{15 I will abundantly bless her provision: I will satisfy her poor with bread.}

\enubox{16 I will also clothe her priests with salvation: and her saints shall shout aloud for joy.}

\enubox{17 There will I make the horn of David to bud: I have ordained a lamp for mine anointed.}

\enubox{18 His enemies will I clothe with shame: but upon himself shall his crown flourish.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 133}

\end{center}


\enubox{1 Behold, how good and how pleasant it is for brethren to dwell together in unity!}

\enubox{2 It is like the precious ointment upon the head, that ran down upon the beard, even Aaron's beard: that went down to the skirts of his garments;}

\enubox{3 As the dew of Hermon, and as the dew that descended upon the mountains of Zion: for there the LORD commanded the blessing, even life for evermore.}

\enubox{\bf Chapter 134}

\enubox{1 Behold, bless ye the LORD, all ye servants of the LORD, which by night stand in the house of the LORD.}

\enubox{2 Lift up your hands in the sanctuary, and bless the LORD.}

\enubox{3 The LORD that made heaven and earth bless thee out of Zion.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 135}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the name of the LORD; praise him, O ye servants of the LORD.}

\enubox{2 Ye that stand in the house of the LORD, in the courts of the house of our God.}

\enubox{3 Praise the LORD; for the LORD is good: sing praises unto his name; for it is pleasant.}

\enubox{4 For the LORD hath chosen Jacob unto himself, and Israel for his peculiar treasure.}

\enubox{5 For I know that the LORD is great, and that our Lord is above all gods.}

\enubox{6 Whatsoever the LORD pleased, that did he in heaven, and in earth, in the seas, and all deep places.}

\enubox{7 He causeth the vapours to ascend from the ends of the earth; he maketh lightnings for the rain; he bringeth the wind out of his treasuries.}

\enubox{8 Who smote the firstborn of Egypt, both of man and beast.}

\enubox{9 Who sent tokens and wonders into the midst of thee, O Egypt, upon Pharaoh, and upon all his servants.}

\enubox{10 Who smote great nations, and slew mighty kings;}

\enubox{11 Sihon king of the Amorites, and Og king of Bashan, and all the kingdoms of Canaan:}

\enubox{12 And gave their land for an heritage, an heritage unto Israel his people.}

\enubox{13 Thy name, O LORD, endureth for ever; and thy memorial, O LORD, throughout all generations.}

\enubox{14 For the LORD will judge his people, and he will repent himself concerning his servants.}

\enubox{15 The idols of the heathen are silver and gold, the work of men's hands.}

\enubox{16 They have mouths, but they speak not; eyes have they, but they see not;}

\enubox{17 They have ears, but they hear not; neither is there any breath in their mouths.}

\enubox{18 They that make them are like unto them: so is every one that trusteth in them.}

\enubox{19 Bless the LORD, O house of Israel: bless the LORD, O house of Aaron:}

\enubox{20 Bless the LORD, O house of Levi: ye that fear the LORD, bless the LORD.}

\enubox{21 Blessed be the LORD out of Zion, which dwelleth at Jerusalem. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 136}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M509x515S18720491x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O give thanks unto the LORD; for he is good: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{2 O give thanks unto the God of gods: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{3 O give thanks to the Lord of lords: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{4 To him who alone doeth great wonders: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{5 To him that by wisdom made the heavens: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{6 To him that stretched out the earth above the waters: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{7 To him that made great lights: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{8 The sun to rule by day: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{9 The moon and stars to rule by night: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{10 To him that smote Egypt in their firstborn: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{11 And brought out Israel from among them: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{12 With a strong hand, and with a stretched out arm: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{13 To him which divided the Red sea into parts: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{14 And made Israel to pass through the midst of it: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{15 But overthrew Pharaoh and his host in the Red sea: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{16 To him which led his people through the wilderness: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{17 To him which smote great kings: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{18 And slew famous kings: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{19 Sihon king of the Amorites: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{20 And Og the king of Bashan: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{21 And gave their land for an heritage: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{22 Even an heritage unto Israel his servant: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{23 Who remembered us in our low estate: for his mercy endureth for ever:}

\enubox{24 And hath redeemed us from our enemies: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{25 Who giveth food to all flesh: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\enubox{26 O give thanks unto the God of heaven: for his mercy endureth for ever.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 137}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x514S1a520490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 By the rivers of Babylon, there we sat down, yea, we wept, when we remembered Zion.}

\enubox{2 We hanged our harps upon the willows in the midst thereof.}

\enubox{3 For there they that carried us away captive required of us a song; and they that wasted us required of us mirth, saying, Sing us one of the songs of Zion.}

\enubox{4 How shall we sing the LORD's song in a strange land?}

\enubox{5 If I forget thee, O Jerusalem, let my right hand forget her cunning.}

\enubox{6 If I do not remember thee, let my tongue cleave to the roof of my mouth; if I prefer not Jerusalem above my chief joy.}

\enubox{7 Remember, O LORD, the children of Edom in the day of Jerusalem; who said, Rase it, rase it, even to the foundation thereof.}

\enubox{8 O daughter of Babylon, who art to be destroyed; happy shall he be, that rewardeth thee as thou hast served us.}

\enubox{9 Happy shall he be, that taketh and dasheth thy little ones against the stones.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 138}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x514S1bb20490x486 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I will praise thee with my whole heart: before the gods will I sing praise unto thee.}

\enubox{2 I will worship toward thy holy temple, and praise thy name for thy lovingkindness and for thy truth: for thou hast magnified thy word above all thy name.}

\enubox{3 In the day when I cried thou answeredst me, and strengthenedst me with strength in my soul.}

\enubox{4 All the kings of the earth shall praise thee, O LORD, when they hear the words of thy mouth.}

\enubox{5 Yea, they shall sing in the ways of the LORD: for great is the glory of the LORD.}

\enubox{6 Though the LORD be high, yet hath he respect unto the lowly: but the proud he knoweth afar off.}

\enubox{7 Though I walk in the midst of trouble, thou wilt revive me: thou shalt stretch forth thine hand against the wrath of mine enemies, and thy right hand shall save me.}

\enubox{8 The LORD will perfect that which concerneth me: thy mercy, O LORD, endureth for ever: forsake not the works of thine own hands.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 139}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 M511x515S1ce20489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 O lord, thou hast searched me, and known me.}

\enubox{2 Thou knowest my downsitting and mine uprising, thou understandest my thought afar off.}

\enubox{3 Thou compassest my path and my lying down, and art acquainted with all my ways.}

\enubox{4 For there is not a word in my tongue, but, lo, O LORD, thou knowest it altogether.}

\enubox{5 Thou hast beset me behind and before, and laid thine hand upon me.}

\enubox{6 Such knowledge is too wonderful for me; it is high, I cannot attain unto it.}

\enubox{7 Whither shall I go from thy spirit? or whither shall I flee from thy presence?}

\enubox{8 If I ascend up into heaven, thou art there: if I make my bed in hell, behold, thou art there.}

\enubox{9 If I take the wings of the morning, and dwell in the uttermost parts of the sea;}

\enubox{10 Even there shall thy hand lead me, and thy right hand shall hold me.}

\enubox{11 If I say, Surely the darkness shall cover me; even the night shall be light about me.}

\enubox{12 Yea, the darkness hideth not from thee; but the night shineth as the day: the darkness and the light are both alike to thee.}

\enubox{13 For thou hast possessed my reins: thou hast covered me in my mother's womb.}

\enubox{14 I will praise thee; for I am fearfully and wonderfully made: marvellous are thy works; and that my soul knoweth right well.}

\enubox{15 My substance was not hid from thee, when I was made in secret, and curiously wrought in the lowest parts of the earth.}

\enubox{16 Thine eyes did see my substance, yet being unperfect; and in thy book all my members were written, which in continuance were fashioned, when as yet there was none of them.}

\enubox{17 How precious also are thy thoughts unto me, O God! how great is the sum of them!}

\enubox{18 If I should count them, they are more in number than the sand: when I awake, I am still with thee.}

\enubox{19 Surely thou wilt slay the wicked, O God: depart from me therefore, ye bloody men.}

\enubox{20 For they speak against thee wickedly, and thine enemies take thy name in vain.}

\enubox{21 Do not I hate them, O LORD, that hate thee? and am not I grieved with those that rise up against thee?}

\enubox{22 I hate them with perfect hatred: I count them mine enemies.}

\enubox{23 Search me, O God, and know my heart: try me, and know my thoughts:}

\enubox{24 And see if there be any wicked way in me, and lead me in the way everlasting.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 140}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M508x508S17610492x492 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Deliver me, O LORD, from the evil man: preserve me from the violent man;}

\enubox{2 Which imagine mischiefs in their heart; continually are they gathered together for war.}

\enubox{3 They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent; adders' poison is under their lips. Selah.}

\enubox{4 Keep me, O LORD, from the hands of the wicked; preserve me from the violent man; who have purposed to overthrow my goings.}

\enubox{5 The proud have hid a snare for me, and cords; they have spread a net by the wayside; they have set gins for me. Selah.}

\enubox{6 I said unto the LORD, Thou art my God: hear the voice of my supplications, O LORD.}

\enubox{7 O GOD the Lord, the strength of my salvation, thou hast covered my head in the day of battle.}

\enubox{8 Grant not, O LORD, the desires of the wicked: further not his wicked device; lest they exalt themselves. Selah.}

\enubox{9 As for the head of those that compass me about, let the mischief of their own lips cover them.}

\enubox{10 Let burning coals fall upon them: let them be cast into the fire; into deep pits, that they rise not up again.}

\enubox{11 Let not an evil speaker be established in the earth: evil shall hunt the violent man to overthrow him.}

\enubox{12 I know that the LORD will maintain the cause of the afflicted, and the right of the poor.}

\enubox{13 Surely the righteous shall give thanks unto thy name: the upright shall dwell in thy presence.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 142}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M508x515S10e00493x485

\enubox{1 I cried unto the LORD with my voice; with my voice unto the LORD did I make my supplication.}

\enubox{2 I poured out my complaint before him; I shewed before him my trouble.}

\enubox{3 When my spirit was overwhelmed within me, then thou knewest my path. In the way wherein I walked have they privily laid a snare for me.}

\enubox{4 I looked on my right hand, and beheld, but there was no man that would know me: refuge failed me; no man cared for my soul.}

\enubox{5 I cried unto thee, O LORD: I said, Thou art my refuge and my portion in the land of the living.}

\enubox{6 Attend unto my cry; for I am brought very low: deliver me from my persecutors; for they are stronger than I.}

\enubox{7 Bring my soul out of prison, that I may praise thy name: the righteous shall compass me about; for thou shalt deal bountifully with me.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 143}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M512x515S11e00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Hear my prayer, O LORD, give ear to my supplications: in thy faithfulness answer me, and in thy righteousness.}

\enubox{2 And enter not into judgment with thy servant: for in thy sight shall no man living be justified.}

\enubox{3 For the enemy hath persecuted my soul; he hath smitten my life down to the ground; he hath made me to dwell in darkness, as those that have been long dead.}

\enubox{4 Therefore is my spirit overwhelmed within me; my heart within me is desolate.}

\enubox{5 I remember the days of old; I meditate on all thy works; I muse on the work of thy hands.}

\enubox{6 I stretch forth my hands unto thee: my soul thirsteth after thee, as a thirsty land. Selah.}

\enubox{7 Hear me speedily, O LORD: my spirit faileth: hide not thy face from me, lest I be like unto them that go down into the pit.}

\enubox{8 Cause me to hear thy lovingkindness in the morning; for in thee do I trust: cause me to know the way wherein I should walk; for I lift up my soul unto thee.}

\enubox{9 Deliver me, O LORD, from mine enemies: I flee unto thee to hide me.}

\enubox{10 Teach me to do thy will; for thou art my God: thy spirit is good; lead me into the land of uprightness.}

\enubox{11 Quicken me, O LORD, for thy name's sake: for thy righteousness' sake bring my soul out of trouble.}

\enubox{12 And of thy mercy cut off mine enemies, and destroy all them that afflict my soul: for I am thy servant.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 144}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M511x516S14400489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 Blessed be the LORD my strength which teacheth my hands to war, and my fingers to fight:}

\enubox{2 My goodness, and my fortress; my high tower, and my deliverer; my shield, and he in whom I trust; who subdueth my people under me.}

\enubox{3 LORD, what is man, that thou takest knowledge of him! or the son of man, that thou makest account of him!}

\enubox{4 Man is like to vanity: his days are as a shadow that passeth away.}

\enubox{5 Bow thy heavens, O LORD, and come down: touch the mountains, and they shall smoke.}

\enubox{6 Cast forth lightning, and scatter them: shoot out thine arrows, and destroy them.}

\enubox{7 Send thine hand from above; rid me, and deliver me out of great waters, from the hand of strange children;}

\enubox{8 Whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood.}

\enubox{9 I will sing a new song unto thee, O God: upon a psaltery and an instrument of ten strings will I sing praises unto thee.}

\enubox{10 It is he that giveth salvation unto kings: who delivereth David his servant from the hurtful sword.}

\enubox{11 Rid me, and deliver me from the hand of strange children, whose mouth speaketh vanity, and their right hand is a right hand of falsehood:}

\enubox{12 That our sons may be as plants grown up in their youth; that our daughters may be as corner stones, polished after the similitude of a palace:}

\enubox{13 That our garners may be full, affording all manner of store: that our sheep may bring forth thousands and ten thousands in our streets:}

\enubox{14 That our oxen may be strong to labour; that there be no breaking in, nor going out; that there be no complaining in our streets.}

\enubox{15 Happy is that people, that is in such a case: yea, happy is that people, whose God is the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 145}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M512x516S14c00489x485 
\end{center}


\enubox{1 I will extol thee, my God, O king; and I will bless thy name for ever and ever.}

\enubox{2 Every day will I bless thee; and I will praise thy name for ever and ever.}

\enubox{3 Great is the LORD, and greatly to be praised; and his greatness is unsearchable.}

\enubox{4 One generation shall praise thy works to another, and shall declare thy mighty acts.}

\enubox{5 I will speak of the glorious honour of thy majesty, and of thy wondrous works.}

\enubox{6 And men shall speak of the might of thy terrible acts: and I will declare thy greatness.}

\enubox{7 They shall abundantly utter the memory of thy great goodness, and shall sing of thy righteousness.}

\enubox{8 The LORD is gracious, and full of compassion; slow to anger, and of great mercy.}

\enubox{9 The LORD is good to all: and his tender mercies are over all his works.}

\enubox{10 All thy works shall praise thee, O LORD; and thy saints shall bless thee.}

\enubox{11 They shall speak of the glory of thy kingdom, and talk of thy power;}

\enubox{12 To make known to the sons of men his mighty acts, and the glorious majesty of his kingdom.}

\enubox{13 Thy kingdom is an everlasting kingdom, and thy dominion endureth throughout all generations.}

\enubox{14 The LORD upholdeth all that fall, and raiseth up all those that be bowed down.}

\enubox{15 The eyes of all wait upon thee; and thou givest them their meat in due season.}

\enubox{16 Thou openest thine hand, and satisfiest the desire of every living thing.}

\enubox{17 The LORD is righteous in all his ways, and holy in all his works.}

\enubox{18 The LORD is nigh unto all them that call upon him, to all that call upon him in truth.}

\enubox{19 He will fulfil the desire of them that fear him: he also will hear their cry, and will save them.}

\enubox{20 The LORD preserveth all them that love him: but all the wicked will he destroy.}

\enubox{21 My mouth shall speak the praise of the LORD: and let all flesh bless his holy name for ever and ever.}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Praise the LORD, O my soul.}

\enubox{2 While I live will I praise the LORD: I will sing praises unto my God while I have any being.}

\enubox{3 Put not your trust in princes, nor in the son of man, in whom there is no help.}

\enubox{4 His breath goeth forth, he returneth to his earth; in that very day his thoughts perish.}

\enubox{5 Happy is he that hath the God of Jacob for his help, whose hope is in the LORD his God:}

\enubox{6 Which made heaven, and earth, the sea, and all that therein is: which keepeth truth for ever:}

\enubox{7 Which executeth judgment for the oppressed: which giveth food to the hungry. The LORD looseth the prisoners:}

\enubox{8 The LORD openeth the eyes of the blind: the LORD raiseth them that are bowed down: the LORD loveth the righteous:}

\enubox{9 The LORD preserveth the strangers; he relieveth the fatherless and widow: but the way of the wicked he turneth upside down.}

\enubox{10 The LORD shall reign for ever, even thy God, O Zion, unto all generations. Praise ye the LORD.}

\begin{center}
\enubox{\bf Chapter 147}
M517x530S15a48484x471S16d40499x475S22b04501x500 M519x515S16d20502x495S10020481x485 M511x516S14400489x485 M511x514S1a520490x486

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD: for it is good to sing praises unto our God; for it is pleasant; and praise is comely.}

\enubox{2 The LORD doth build up Jerusalem: he gathereth together the outcasts of Israel.}

\enubox{3 He healeth the broken in heart, and bindeth up their wounds.}

\enubox{4 He telleth the number of the stars; he calleth them all by their names.}

\enubox{5 Great is our Lord, and of great power: his understanding is infinite.}

\enubox{6 The LORD lifteth up the meek: he casteth the wicked down to the ground.}

\enubox{7 Sing unto the LORD with thanksgiving; sing praise upon the harp unto our God:}

\enubox{8 Who covereth the heaven with clouds, who prepareth rain for the earth, who maketh grass to grow upon the mountains.}

\enubox{9 He giveth to the beast his food, and to the young ravens which cry.}

\enubox{10 He delighteth not in the strength of the horse: he taketh not pleasure in the legs of a man.}

\enubox{11 The LORD taketh pleasure in them that fear him, in those that hope in his mercy.}

\enubox{12 Praise the LORD, O Jerusalem; praise thy God, O Zion.}

\enubox{13 For he hath strengthened the bars of thy gates; he hath blessed thy children within thee.}

\enubox{14 He maketh peace in thy borders, and filleth thee with the finest of the wheat.}

\enubox{15 He sendeth forth his commandment upon earth: his word runneth very swiftly.}

\enubox{16 He giveth snow like wool: he scattereth the hoarfrost like ashes.}

\enubox{17 He casteth forth his ice like morsels: who can stand before his cold?}

\enubox{18 He sendeth out his word, and melteth them: he causeth his wind to blow, and the waters flow.}

\enubox{19 He sheweth his word unto Jacob, his statutes and his judgments unto Israel.}

\enubox{20 He hath not dealt so with any nation: and as for his judgments, they have not known them. Praise ye the LORD.}

\enubox{\bf Chapter 148}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Praise ye the LORD from the heavens: praise him in the heights.}

\enubox{2 Praise ye him, all his angels: praise ye him, all his hosts.}

\enubox{3 Praise ye him, sun and moon: praise him, all ye stars of light.}

\enubox{4 Praise him, ye heavens of heavens, and ye waters that be above the heavens.}

\enubox{5 Let them praise the name of the LORD: for he commanded, and they were created.}

\enubox{6 He hath also stablished them for ever and ever: he hath made a decree which shall not pass.}

\enubox{7 Praise the LORD from the earth, ye dragons, and all deeps:}

\enubox{8 Fire, and hail; snow, and vapours; stormy wind fulfilling his word:}

\enubox{9 Mountains, and all hills; fruitful trees, and all cedars:}

\enubox{10 Beasts, and all cattle; creeping things, and flying fowl:}

\enubox{11 Kings of the earth, and all people; princes, and all judges of the earth:}

\enubox{12 Both young men, and maidens; old men, and children:}

\enubox{13 Let them praise the name of the LORD: for his name alone is excellent; his glory is above the earth and heaven.}

\enubox{14 He also exalteth the horn of his people, the praise of all his saints; even of the children of Israel, a people near unto him. Praise ye the LORD.}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Sing unto the LORD a new song, and his praise in the congregation of saints.}

\enubox{2 Let Israel rejoice in him that made him: let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.}

\enubox{3 Let them praise his name in the dance: let them sing praises unto him with the timbrel and harp.}

\enubox{4 For the LORD taketh pleasure in his people: he will beautify the meek with salvation.}

\enubox{1 Praise ye the LORD. Praise God in his sanctuary: praise him in the firmament of his power.}

\enubox{2 Praise him for his mighty acts: praise him according to his excellent greatness.}

\enubox{3 Praise him with the sound of the trumpet: praise him with the psaltery and harp.}

\enubox{4 Praise him with the timbrel and dance: praise him with stringed instruments and organs.}

\enubox{5 Praise him upon the loud cymbals: praise him upon the high sounding cymbals.}

\enubox{6 Let every thing that hath breath praise the LORD. Praise ye the LORD.}
